### [1] [PhysX-Omni: Unified Simulation-Ready Physical 3D Generation for Rigid, Deformable, and Articulated Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21572)
*Ziang Cao,Yinghao Liu,Haitian Li,Runmao Yao,Fangzhou Hong,Zhaoxi Chen,Liang Pan,Ziwei Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PhysX-Omni 提出一个统一的仿真就绪物理 3D 资产生成框架，可覆盖刚体、可变形体和关节物体等多类资产，并兼具生成与理解能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 3D 生成方法往往忽略物理属性，或仅适用于单一资产类别，难以满足具身智能、机器人学习和物理仿真等下游任务对通用仿真就绪 3D 资产的需求。

Method: 作者提出 PhysX-Omni：一是设计面向视觉语言模型的高效几何表示，能够直接编码高分辨率 3D 结构且无需压缩；二是构建通用仿真就绪 3D 数据集 PhysXVerse，覆盖室内外多种类别；三是提出 PhysX-Bench，从几何、绝对尺度、材质、可供性、运动学和功能描述六个属性评估生成与理解能力。

Result: 基于常规指标和 PhysX-Bench 的实验表明，PhysX-Omni 在物理 3D 资产生成和理解方面表现较强；额外实验还验证了其在仿真就绪场景生成和机器人策略学习中的应用潜力。

Conclusion: PhysX-Omni 通过统一框架、通用数据集和综合评测基准推进了仿真就绪物理 3D 生成，有望促进具身 AI、机器人和基于物理的仿真等应用发展。

Abstract: Simulation-ready physical 3D assets have emerged as a promising direction owing to their broad applicability in downstream tasks. However, most existing 3D generation methods either neglect physical properties or are limited to a single asset category, e.g., rigid, deformable, or articulated objects. To address these limitations, we introduce PhysX-Omni, a unified framework for simulation-ready physical 3D generation across diverse asset types. Specifically, we develop a novel and efficient geometry representation tailored for Vision-Language Models, which directly encodes high-resolution 3D structures without compression, significantly improving generation performance. In addition, we construct the first general simulation-ready 3D dataset, PhysXVerse, covering diverse indoor and outdoor categories. Furthermore, to comprehensively and flexibly evaluate both generative and understanding capabilities in the wild, we propose PhysX-Bench, which encompasses six key attributes: geometry, absolute scale, material, affordance, kinematics, and function description. Extensive experiments with conventional metrics and PhysX-Bench show that PhysX-Omni performs strongly in both generation and understanding. Moreover, additional studies further validate the potential of PhysX-Omni for applications in simulation-ready scene generation and robotic policy learning. We believe PhysX-Omni can significantly advance a wide range of downstream applications, particularly in embodied AI and physics-based simulation.

</details>


### [2] [Lens: Rethinking Training Efficiency for Foundational Text-to-Image Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21573)
*Dong Chen,Fangyun Wei,Ziyu Wan,Dongdong Chen,Jiawei Zhang,Jinjing Zhao,Sirui Zhang,Yang Yue,Zhiyang Liang,Baining Guo,Chong Luo,Jianmin Bao,Ji Li,Lei Shi,Qinhong Yang,Xiuyu Wu,Xuelu Feng,Yan Lu,Yanchen Dong,Yitong Wang,Yunuo Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Lens 是一个 3.8B 参数的文本到图像模型，以显著更低训练算力达到或超过更大规模模型的表现，并支持高分辨率、多宽高比和多语言提示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高性能 T2I 模型通常依赖超过 6B 参数规模和大量训练算力，训练与推理成本高。该工作旨在通过更高效的数据、架构和后训练策略，在较小模型规模下获得竞争性生成质量与泛化能力。

Method: 方法包括：构建 Lens-800M 高信息密度图文数据集，使用 GPT-4.1 生成平均约 109 词的密集描述；在训练批次中混合多分辨率和多宽高比图像；采用语义 VAE 与强语言编码器提升潜表示质量、收敛速度和多语言泛化；预训练后使用基于分类体系提示和结构化奖励规则的强化学习优化；引入 reasoner 模块和免训练系统提示搜索增强用户意图对齐；通过蒸馏实现 4 步快速推理。

Result: Lens 在多项基准上与超过 6B 参数的先进模型竞争，部分场景表现更优；相较 Z-Image 仅需约 19.3% 的训练算力。模型支持 1:2 到 2:1 任意宽高比、最高 1440^2 分辨率，并支持多种常用语言提示。3.8B 基础版在单张 NVIDIA H100 上生成 1024^2 图像需 3.15 秒，蒸馏 turbo 版 4 步生成仅需 0.84 秒。

Conclusion: 该论文表明，通过提升数据语义密度、优化视觉覆盖、改进潜空间与语言编码、结合强化学习和蒸馏加速，小规模 T2I 模型也能实现高质量、高效率和较强泛化能力，为降低生成模型训练与部署成本提供了有效路径。

Abstract: We introduce Lens, a 3.8B-parameter T2I model that achieves performance competitive with, and in several cases surpassing, state-of-the-art models with more than 6B parameters across various benchmarks, while requiring significantly less training compute. For example, Lens requires only about 19.3% of the training compute used by Z-Image. The training efficiency of Lens stems from two key strategies beyond its compact model size. First, we maximize data information density per training batch by (i) training on Lens-800M, a dataset of 800M densely captioned image-text pairs whose captions are generated by GPT-4.1 and contain approximately 109 words on average, providing richer semantic supervision than conventional short captions, and (ii) constructing each batch from images with multiple resolutions and diverse aspect ratios, thereby enlarging the effective visual coverage of each optimization step. Second, we improve convergence speed through careful architectural choices, including adopting a semantic VAE that provides better latent representations and employing a strong language encoder that accelerates optimization while enabling multilingual generalization from English-only training data. After pre-training, we apply RL with taxonomy-driven prompts (Lens-RL-8K) and structured reward rubrics to suppress artifacts and improve visual quality, a reasoner module with training-free system prompt search to better align user requests with the model, and distillation-based acceleration for 4-step inference. Through efficient training and systematic optimization, Lens generalizes to arbitrary aspect ratios from 1:2 to 2:1 and resolutions up to 1440^2, and supports prompts in several commonly used languages. Thanks to its compact size, Lens generates a 1024^2 image in 3.15 seconds on a single NVIDIA H100 GPU, while its distilled turbo version performs 4-step generation in 0.84 seconds.

</details>


### [3] [GenEvolve: Self-Evolving Image Generation Agents via Tool-Orchestrated Visual Experience Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21605)
*Sixiang Chen,Zhaohu Xing,Tian Ye,Xinyu Geng,Yunlong Lin,Jianyu Lai,Xuanhua He,Fuxiang Zhai,Jialin Gao,Lei Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 GenEvolve，一个面向开放式图像生成的自进化智能体框架，通过工具编排轨迹与视觉经验蒸馏提升复杂生成请求下的工具使用、参考选择和提示构建能力，并在多个基准上取得领先效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放式图像生成已不再是简单的文本到图像任务。高质量生成往往需要智能体结合模型内部生成能力与外部资源，应对多样、复杂且要求更高的生成需求。现有智能体式图像生成方法多依赖图像级标量奖励，监督信号稀疏，难以有效学习搜索策略、知识调用、参考选择和提示构造。

Method: 作者提出 GenEvolve，基于 Tool-Orchestrated Visual Experience Distillation。每次生成尝试被建模为工具编排轨迹，智能体会收集证据、选择参考、调用生成技能，并组合成提示-参考程序。框架比较同一请求下多条轨迹，将最佳与最差轨迹之间的差异抽象为结构化视觉经验，并仅提供给特权教师分支；随后通过类似 on-policy 自蒸馏的方式，以密集 token 级监督训练学生分支，使其内化更优的搜索、知识激活、参考选择和提示构建能力。作者还构建了 GenEvolve-Data 与 GenEvolve-Bench。

Result: 实验在公开基准和新构建的 GenEvolve-Bench 上显示，GenEvolve 相比强基线获得显著提升，并在当前图像生成框架中达到 state-of-the-art 表现。

Conclusion: GenEvolve 表明，将多轨迹比较得到的结构化视觉经验用于蒸馏，可以比单纯依赖图像级奖励更有效地训练通用图像生成智能体，提升其在复杂开放式生成任务中的工具使用与生成规划能力。

Abstract: Open-ended image generation is no longer a simple prompt-to-image problem. High-quality generation often requires an agent to combine a model's internal generative ability with external resources. As requests become more diverse and demanding, we aim to develop a general image-generation agent that can self-evolve through trajectories and use tools more effectively across varied generation challenges. To this end, we propose GenEvolve, a self-evolving framework based on Tool-Orchestrated Visual Experience Distillation. In GenEvolve, each generation attempt is modeled as a tool-orchestrated trajectory, where the agent gathers evidence, selects references, invokes generation skills, and composes them into a prompt-reference program. Unlike existing agentic generation methods that mainly rely on image-level scalar rewards, GenEvolve compares multiple trajectories for the same request and abstracts best-worst differences into structured visual experience, provided only to a privileged teacher branch. Inspired by on-policy self-distillation, Visual Experience Distillation provides dense token-level supervision, helping the student internalize better search, knowledge activation, reference selection, and prompt construction. We further construct GenEvolve-Data and GenEvolve-Bench. Experiments on public benchmarks and GenEvolve-Bench show substantial gains over strong baselines, achieving state-of-the-art performance among current image-generation frameworks. Our website is as follows: https://ephemeral182.github.io/GenEvolve/

</details>


### [4] [Flat-Pack Bench: Evaluating Spatio-Temporal Understanding in Large Vision-Language Models through Furniture Assembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21625)
*Aditya Chetan,Eric Cai,Peeyush Kushwaha,Bharath Raj Nagoor Kani,Utkarsh Mall,Qianqian Wang,Noah Snavely,Bharath Hariharan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Flat-Pack Bench 是一个面向家具组装视频的细粒度时空理解基准，用于评估大视觉语言模型在动作顺序、状态定位、部件配合与跟踪等任务上的能力；实验显示现有先进模型在细粒度时空推理方面仍明显不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频理解基准多关注动作分类、分割、字幕生成、检索等粗粒度任务，且常依赖易于语言识别的实体，难以评估真实复杂场景中所需的逐步、细粒度时空理解能力。家具组装、烹饪等应用需要模型理解步骤顺序、物体状态变化、空间接触关系和部件交互，因此需要新的评测基准。

Method: 作者提出 Flat-Pack Bench，以家具组装任务为核心，构建多项细粒度评测任务，包括组装动作的时间排序、组装状态的时间定位、部件配合关系理解以及目标跟踪。基准采用多项选择题形式，并结合视觉提示标注相关部件，作为细粒度问题的参考。

Result: 实验表明，当前最先进的大视觉语言模型在该基准上的表现较弱，尤其难以有效利用视频中的时间信息，目标跟踪能力有限，并且对部件接触、配合等空间交互关系理解不足。

Conclusion: Flat-Pack Bench 揭示了现有 LVLM 在细粒度时空推理上的关键短板，说明未来视频理解模型需要更强的时间建模、空间关系理解、物体状态追踪和物理交互推理能力。

Abstract: The emergence of Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) has significantly advanced video understanding capabilities. However, existing benchmarks focus predominantly on coarse-grained tasks such as action segmentation, classification, captioning, and retrieval. Furthermore, these benchmarks often rely on entities that can be easily identified verbally, like household objects, animals, human subjects, etc., limiting their applicability to complex, in-the-wild video scenarios. But, many applications such as furniture assembly, cooking, etc., require step-by-step fine-grained spatio-temporal understanding of the video, which is not sufficiently evaluated in current benchmarks. To address this gap, we introduce Flat-Pack Bench, a novel benchmark centered on furniture assembly tasks. Our benchmark evaluates LVLMs on nuanced tasks, including temporal ordering of assembly actions, temporal localization of assembly state, understanding part mating, and tracking, using multiple-choice questions paired with visual prompts highlighting relevant parts as references for fine-grained questions. Our experiments reveal that state-of-the-art LVLMs struggle significantly with fine-grained spatio-temporal reasoning, highlighting their limitations in effectively leveraging temporal information from videos, limited tracking ability, and understanding of spatial interactions like physical contact.

</details>


### [5] [Ablate-to-Validate: Are Vision-Language Models Really Using Continuous Thought Tokens?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21642)
*Tianyi Zhang,Mahtab Bigverdi,Ranjay Krishna*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出 Ablate-to-Validate 诊断原则及 Token Replacement Test（TRT），用于检验视觉语言模型中的连续/潜在非文本 token 是否真正承载并被用于推理；实验显示，许多准确率提升即使在 token 内容被破坏或替换后仍保留，说明提升不等同于真实“视觉思考”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 VLM 常通过引入连续或潜在非文本 token 来支持所谓“视觉思考”，并报告任务准确率提升。但准确率提升可能来自上下文长度增加、特殊 token 锚定、训练正则化等混杂因素，不能证明模型实际利用了这些 token 的内容进行推理。因此需要一种能隔离 token 内容贡献的诊断方法。

Method: 作者形式化提出 Ablate-to-Validate 原则，并实现为 Token Replacement Test（TRT）。TRT 在固定提示、图像、token 预算和解码设置的条件下，将中间 token 替换为零向量、随机 token、首个 token 重复或 oracle 替代项，以判断性能是否依赖 token 内容。实验包括受控的相对深度推理测试，使用 LLaVA-13B 与 Qwen2.5-VL-3B，在 SigLIP2、CLIP、DINOv2 等冻结编码器和不同 token 预算下训练模型预测/消费连续或离散深度 span；同时也将 TRT 应用于 Mirage、Mull-Tokens、CoVT 等现成视觉思考系统，在 BLINK、VSP、CV-Bench 上评估。

Result: 跨模型、编码器、token 形式、token 预算和多个基准数据集的结果显示，准确率提升往往是误导性的：即使潜在 token 的内容被置零、随机化或重复替换，模型仍保留大部分性能增益。这表明许多系统的收益更多来自 token 的存在或相关训练/结构效应，而非真正利用 token 内容作为信息瓶颈进行推理。

Conclusion: 论文认为，引入潜在视觉思考通道并不意味着模型真正使用该通道进行内容依赖的推理。TRT 可作为评估连续 thought token 或 latent token 方法的标准诊断工具，应与传统准确率指标共同报告，以区分表面性能提升和真实的 latent-token reasoning。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly augmented with continuous or latent non-textual tokens intended to support "visual thinking." Despite improved task accuracy, this alone does not show that models actually use these tokens for reasoning -- gains may arise from confounds such as added context length, special-token anchoring, or training-time regularization. We formalize a diagnostic principle, Ablate-to-Validate, for testing whether latent-token content is genuinely utilized, and instantiate it as the Token Replacement Test (TRT), a standardized suite of content-replacement ablations. TRT holds the prompt, image, token budget, and decoding fixed while replacing intermediate tokens with zero, random, first-repeat, or oracle alternatives, isolating whether performance depends on token content or merely on token presence. As a controlled testbed, we study relative depth reasoning with LLaVA-13B and Qwen2.5-VL-3B, training models to predict and consume continuous or discrete depth spans across multiple frozen encoders (SigLIP2, CLIP, DINOv2) and token budgets. We additionally apply TRT to three off-the-shelf visual-thinking systems (Mirage, Mull-Tokens, CoVT) on BLINK, VSP, and CV-Bench. Across all settings, accuracy gains are a misleading proxy for latent-token reasoning: VLMs retain most improvement even when token content is corrupted or replaced, revealing a persistent gap between having a latent channel and using it as an information bottleneck. We recommend TRT as a standard diagnostic alongside accuracy for any method introducing continuous thought tokens.

</details>


### [6] [Look-Closer-Then-Diagnose: Confidence-Aware Ultrasound VQA via Active Zooming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21652)
*Yue Zhou,Erxuan Wu,Yikang Sun,Hongjoo Lee,Yuan Bi,Huixiong Xu,Zhongliang Jiang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出面向超声医疗视觉问答的框架，通过“先缩放后诊断”和不确定性感知奖励，使模型更贴近超声医师的认知流程，并显著提升病灶定位能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医学视觉语言模型在超声场景表现不足：一方面缺少诊断前主动聚焦病灶区域的交互式机制；另一方面通常将标注视为无偏真值，忽略超声诊断中由主观性导致的模糊性和不确定性。

Method: 作者提出结构化的 Zoom-then-Diagnose 范式，模拟超声医师先搜索并放大病灶、再进行诊断推理的流程；同时在 Group Relative Policy Optimization 框架中引入基于随机组内 rollout 的不确定性感知奖励，用预测一致性近似模型置信度，从而在明确样本上强化正确预测、在模糊样本上保持谨慎。

Result: 在肝脏、乳腺和甲状腺超声数据集上的实验显示，该框架将病灶定位性能提升了 39.3%，表明模型学会了主动聚焦病灶并进行诊断。

Conclusion: 该工作通过结合病灶聚焦交互流程与不确定性感知优化，使医学 VLM 更符合超声诊断工作流，并提升了超声视觉问答中的定位与诊断可靠性。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have significantly advanced medical visual question answering, yet their performance in ultrasound remains suboptimal. In clinical practice, sonographers explicitly focus on lesion regions to formulate reports, though diagnostic interpretations sometimes vary due to inherent subjectivity. However, existing VLMs are not explicitly structured to interactively zoom into lesions prior to diagnosis; moreover, they typically treat annotations as unbiased ground truths, failing to account for their inherent subjectivity and ambiguity. In this paper, we propose a framework specifically designed to consider the sonographer's cognitive workflow. We first introduce a structured Zoom-then-Diagnose paradigm, which replicates the interactive search process to enable lesion-focused reasoning. Furthermore, within the Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) framework, we introduce an uncertainty-aware reward derived from stochastic group-wise rollouts to estimate prediction consistency as a proxy for model confidence. Together, these two components encourage the model to reinforce accurate predictions on clear cases while remaining cautious under ambiguity. Experiments across liver, breast, and thyroid datasets show that our framework improves lesion localization by 39.3\%, demonstrating that our model has learned the ability to actively look closer and diagnose.

</details>


### [7] [MRecover: A Conditional Generative Model for Recovering Motion-Corrupted MR images Using AI Generated Contrast](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21669)
*Jinghang Li,Tales Santini,Courtney Clark,Bruno de Almeida,Cong Chu,Salem Alkhateeb,Andrea Sajewski,Jacob Berardinelli,Hecheng Jin,Tobias Campos,Jeremy J. Berardo,Joseph Mettenburg,Ariel Gildengers,Howard J. Aizenstein,Minjie Wu,Tamer S. Ibrahim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出 MRecover：一种条件生成模型，可由常规 T1w MRI 合成高分辨率 T2w TSE 图像，用于海马亚区分割，并能缓解运动伪影导致的数据损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海马亚区分割通常依赖高分辨率 T2w TSE MRI，但该序列容易受到运动伪影影响，导致大量受试者数据在质控后不可用；因此需要一种利用更常规、可获得性更高的 T1w 图像来恢复或替代 TSE 图像的方法。

Method: 作者开发了条件生成模型 MRecover，将 T1w 图像合成为 TSE 图像，并引入自回归切片条件机制以增强体数据的一致性。模型在 7T MRI 数据上训练，并在域内 7T 测试集及域外 3T 数据上评估图像相似性、海马亚区体积一致性和下游诊断组差异分析效果。

Result: 模型在域内测试中取得较高保真度（SSIM=0.84，FSIM=0.94）；在域外 3T 数据上，合成图像与真实采集图像得到的亚区体积高度相关（r=0.87–0.97）。在受运动影响的 ADNI3 数据集中，合成图像使可分析受试者数量增加 31.8%（593 vs 450），并因样本量扩大而提升海马亚区萎缩诊断组差异的效应量。

Conclusion: MRecover 可有效从 T1w MRI 合成适用于海马亚区分割的 TSE 图像，在保持较好体积测量一致性的同时显著减少运动伪影造成的数据流失，提升下游神经影像统计分析的可用样本量和检测效能。

Abstract: Hippocampal subfield segmentation requires high-resolution T2w turbo spin echo (TSE) MRI, yet this sequence is susceptible to motion artifacts, leading to substantial data loss. We developed a conditional generative model (MRecover) that synthesizes routinely acquired T1w images to create TSE images with autoregressive slice conditioning for volumetric consistency. Trained on 7T MRI data (n=577), the model achieved high in-domain fidelity (n=148, SSIM=0.84, FSIM=0.94) and generalized well to out-of-domain 3T data: subfield volumes from synthesized and the as-acquired images closely matched: (n=416, r=0.87-0.97) and yielded 31.8% more analyzable subjects in the motion-affected ADNI3 dataset after quality control (593 vs 450). The synthesized images also achieved larger effect sizes due to increasing the sample size for diagnostic group differences in hippocampal subfield atrophy (whole hippocampus $ε^2$= 0.121-0.100 vs. 0.086-0.062, left-right hemispheres). Project page: https://jinghangli98.github.io/MRecover/

</details>


### [8] [AVI-HT: Adaptive Vision-IMU Fusion for 3D Hand Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21714)
*Ziyi Kou,Ankit Kumar,Mia Huang,Taylor Niehues,Vatsal Mehta,Ergys Ristani,Li Guan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AVI-HT是一种自适应视觉-IMU融合的3D手部姿态跟踪方法，在严重遮挡的手-物交互场景中显著提升精度与可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单纯依赖自我中心视觉进行3D手部姿态跟踪时，手-物交互中的严重遮挡会导致估计不稳定；而手套上的IMU信号可提供互补运动信息，因此需要一种能自适应融合视觉与多IMU传感器信息的方法。

Method: 作者构建同步的多模态训练数据，将穿戴式视觉-IMU传感器流与动捕系统提供的3D手部姿态真值配对；提出跨传感器深度注意力机制，根据场景与传感器状态动态调节视觉和各个IMU传感器的可信度，并在UmeTrack与MANO两种手模型下进行评估。

Result: 在DexGloveHOI数据集上，AVI-HT相较基线将平均关键点误差降低16.1%，其腕部对齐变体降低24.2%；消融实验揭示了不同活动中各手指IMU的贡献，并分析了模型对IMU噪声和视觉-IMU时间错位的敏感性。

Conclusion: AVI-HT证明了自适应跨模态融合对复杂真实手-物交互中的3D手部跟踪具有明显优势，尤其适用于视觉遮挡严重的场景。

Abstract: We present AVI-HT, an adaptive visual-IMU fusion approach for tracking 3D hand poses by jointly modeling the egocentric image with on-glove 6-DoF IMU signals. AVI-HT achieves significantly improved accuracy and availability, particularly in hand-object interaction (HOI) scenarios involving heavy visual occlusion. Two complementary ingredients underpin its success: (1) synchronized multi-modal training data pairing on-body vision-IMU sensor streams with ground-truth 3D hand poses from a motion-capture system, and (2) a cross-sensor deep attention mechanism that adaptively modulates the trust assigned to the vision and individual IMU sensors. To evaluate AVI-HT in real-world settings, we conduct extensive experiments on our DexGloveHOI dataset that consists of 100K+ pairwise vision-IMU samples with synchronized 3D annotated poses, in which users manipulate a variety of objects during daily tasks. We compare against multiple single- and multi-modal tracking approaches under two hand models (UmeTrack, MANO). The results show that AVI-HT reduces mean keypoint error by 16.1% and its wrist-aligned variant by 24.2% over the baselines. Ablation studies further reveal the per-finger contribution of IMU sensors across activity types, and the model's sensitivity to IMU noise and temporal misalignment in vision-IMU fusion.

We propose a new learned metric that tackles the aforementioned challenges, based on a lightweight cross-encoder that is initialized from a visual question-answering model checkpoint, balancing a strong weight initialization with computational efficiency. Our training scheme uses a carefully assembled data mixture for supervised learning, featuring adversarial LLM-based data augmentations to enhance model sensitivity to fine-grained visual-linguistic errors. We also introduce a new benchmark designed to assess detailed captioning evaluation across diverse scenarios. ### [11] [BodyReLux: Temporally Consistent Full-Body Video Relighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21766)

Method: 论文构建混合像素对齐视频重光照数据集，结合静态 OLAT 采集与一种动态表演采集方式：快速交错两组平滑变化的光照序列，并利用人眼闪烁融合阈值避免可见频闪。在模型上，从预训练文本到视频模型初始化，利用生成先验提升视频质量；提出将每个光源表示为 token 的光照条件机制，并通过 masked attention 对光照序列建模，以支持动态光照控制；同时设计数据增强流程增强鲁棒性。

Abstract: Being able to relight human performance is a fundamental task for post production and content creation. We present BodyReLux, a subject-specific video diffusion-based framework for relighting full-body human performances in a temporally consistent way. Our model is trained on a hybrid dataset of pixel-aligned video relighting pairs, covering a diverse combination of lighting conditions, performances and viewpoints. To acquire such dataset, we combine traditional static One-Light-at-a-Time (OLAT) capture and a novel dynamic performance capture in which two smoothly varying lighting sequences are rapidly interleaved. Because the lighting operates above the human flicker-fusion threshold, the interleaving does not appear to strobe. We train our video relighting model from a pretrained text-to-video model to fully leverage the generative priors for producing high quality videos. To achieve accurate lighting control, we introduce a new lighting conditioning method that represents each light source as a token. We further condition on sequences of lighting using masked attention to support dynamic lighting control. Together with a carefully designed data augmentation pipeline, we achieve photorealistic, robust, and temporally consistent video relighting of subject-specific human performances.

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出 SceneGraphGrounder，将零样本 3D 视觉定位转化为重建 3D 场景图上的结构化图匹配问题，以提升多视角一致性与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于视觉-语言模型的方法虽在零样本 3D grounding 中表现较好，但常依赖视角相关推理或隐式表示，导致空间一致性不足，并且在处理组合式语言查询时缺乏可解释性。

Method: 方法先通过视觉标记提示策略，使 VLM 从 2D 视图中推断物体间关系；随后将这些关系提升并整合为持久化 3D 场景图，编码空间与语义关系。对输入语言查询构建查询图，并与场景图进行带约束的图对齐，实现结构化匹配。

Result: 在 ScanRefer 基准上，该方法在仅使用 RGB-D 输入的条件下，在零样本方法中取得有竞争力的性能；同时在移动机器人真实部署中验证了其在长时程物理环境中的稳健空间推理能力。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，将 3D grounding 显式建模为场景图匹配能够增强多视角一致性、推理可解释性和真实环境适用性，是零样本 3D 视觉语言定位的一种有前景的方向。

Abstract: Zero-shot 3D visual grounding requires localizing objects in unstructured environments from free-form natural language. Recent vision-language model (VLM) approaches achieve promising results but rely on view-dependent reasoning or implicit representations, limiting spatial consistency and interpretability for compositional queries. We propose SceneGraphGrounder, a framework that reformulates 3D grounding as structured graph matching over a reconstructed 3D scene graph. To enable this formulation, we introduce a visual marker prompting strategy that enables a VLM to infer object-object relationships from 2D views, which are subsequently lifted into a persistent 3D scene graph encoding both spatial and semantic relations. Given a query, we construct a query graph and perform constrained alignment with the scene graph, ensuring multi-view consistency and interpretable reasoning. Experiments on the ScanRefer benchmark demonstrate that our method achieves competitive performance among zero-shot approaches, using only RGB-D inputs. We further validate our framework through real-world deployment on a mobile robot, demonstrating robust spatial reasoning in long-horizon physical environments. We will make our code publicly available upon acceptance.

We address this gap by introducing (1) a benchmark for referential communication in dynamic 3D environments, built from 6.7 hours of egocentric VR interaction with synchronized speech, motion, gaze, and 3D scene geometry, and (2) a two-stage grounding pipeline that explicitly resolves conversational ambiguity before visual localization. ### [15] [CrossVLA: Cross-Paradigm Post-Training and Inference Optimization for Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21854)
*Zhi Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 CrossVLA，对跨范式 VLA 后训练进行经验研究，使 DPO 可用于连续动作 flow-matching 骨干，并系统比较参数高效适配与推理瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 VLA 架构主要分为离散 token 自回归与连续动作 flow-matching 两类，但偏好对齐方法 DPO 主要在自回归 VLA 上研究，缺少面向连续动作范式及跨架构范式的统一后训练分析。

Method: 提出一种替代的 flow-matching 对数概率估计器，使 DPO 无需概率流 ODE 积分即可作用于连续动作模型；比较 LoRA 与 DoRA 作为 VLA DPO 的参数高效层；分析推理阶段 sample_actions 的延迟组成与 K/V 缓存策略；同时在 6000 个 LIBERO 帧上预训练多视角与时间投影头。

Result: DoRA-DPO 相比 OpenVLA SFT 在 LIBERO 4-suite 上平均提升 +10.4 个百分点，分项为 Object +20.0、Long-horizon +11.0、Goal +8.0、Spatial +2.7；Object 任务三种种子均为 38/50，种子方差为 0。推理分析显示去噪循环占 sample_actions 延迟的 78.6%，prefix-K/V 缓存加速上限约 21%，chunk/token 级缓存会使成功率降至 0–80%。预训练投影头达到同任务检索 k-NN recall@1 为 99.5%。

Conclusion: CrossVLA 表明 DPO 可扩展到连续动作 flow-matching VLA，并且 DoRA 是更有效的参数高效对齐方式；同时指出当前 VLA 推理瓶颈主要来自去噪循环，简单 K/V 缓存并不能可靠提升端到端性能。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have rapidly converged on a small set of architectural patterns: discrete-token autoregression (e.g. OpenVLA) and continuous-action flow-matching (e.g. pi-0.5). Yet preference alignment via Direct Preference Optimisation (DPO) -- the de-facto post-training step in language models -- has been studied almost exclusively on autoregressive VLAs. We present CrossVLA, an empirical study of cross-paradigm VLA post-training. Three contributions: (i) a surrogate flow-matching log-probability estimator that lets DPO operate on continuous-action backbones without probability-flow ODE integration; (ii) a head-to-head comparison of LoRA and DoRA as the parameter-efficient layer for VLA DPO, finding DoRA improves over OpenVLA SFT by a mean +10.4 pp across LIBERO 4-suite (600 trials, 3 seeds) -- per-suite +20.0 Object, +11.0 Long-horizon, +8.0 Goal, +2.7 Spatial -- with zero seed variance on Object (38/50 on each of 3 seeds); (iii) an inference-time anatomy showing the denoise loop dominates 78.6% of sample_actions latency and prefix-K/V caching a la VLA-Cache caps at a 21% acceleration ceiling -- both chunk-level and token-level cache strategies degrade success rate to 0-80% in our benchmarks. We further pretrain a multi-view + temporal projection head on 6000 LIBERO frames, achieving 99.5% k-NN recall@1 for same-task retrieval (36x over random), available as a downstream initialisation. All code, ckpts, training logs, and reproduction scripts are open at https://github.com/lz-googlefycy/vla-lab.

### [16] [Two-Stage Multimodal Framework for Emotion Mimicry Intensity Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21869)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该任务需要从真实场景多模态视频中预测六个连续情绪强度维度，具有数据噪声大、模态异质性强和连续回归难度高等挑战，因此需要一个实用、可复现且能有效融合多模态信息的基线方法。

Method: 方法采用分阶段训练策略：先分别训练文本、声学、视觉等模态特定编码器，并加入可选的运动分支；随后通过轻量级回归器融合各模态表示，同时使用模态 dropout 和受控编码器自适应来提升鲁棒性与泛化能力。

Result: 在验证集上，文本-音频-视觉-运动融合模型在扩展 4:1 划分下取得最佳表现，平均 Pearson 相关系数为 0.4722；运动分支仅带来轻微增益。最终测试集平均 Pearson 相关系数为 0.57，团队在 EMI 挑战中排名第三。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，分阶段多模态融合框架能够有效处理情绪模仿强度预测任务，并提供了一个性能较强、实现相对简单且可复现的基线；运动信息的贡献有限但具有进一步分析价值。

Abstract: We present our submission to the Hume-ABAW10 Emotional Mimicry Intensity (EMI) Challenge, which aims to predict six continuous emotion intensity dimensions: Admiration, Amusement, Determination, Empathic Pain, Excitement, and Joy, from in-the-wild multimodal video clips. We propose a staged multimodal framework that combines textual, acoustic, and visual representations, with an optional motion branch. Our approach first trains modality-specific encoders independently and then fuses their learned representations through a lightweight regressor with modality dropout and controlled encoder adaptation. Across our submitted systems, the best validation performance is obtained by the text--audio--vision--motion fusion model under the expanded 4:1 split, achieving an average Pearson correlation of 0.4722. Although the motion branch yields only very slight gains, its behavior can be interesting to study. Our team was placed third in the EMI challenge, achieving an average Pearson correlation of 0.57 for the test set. Overall, we provide a practical and reproducible baseline for EMI prediction.

### [17] [Thermo-VL: Extending Vision-Language Models to Thermal Infrared Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21882)

Result: 实验显示，Thermo-VL 在热红外-only 以及 RGB+thermal 的低光照、跨光谱推理任务上取得明显提升，证明 prompt-conditioned 多光谱融合有效。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，在保持预训练 RGB-语言接口稳定的同时，引入文本条件化的热红外融合能够增强 VLM 在低照度和跨光谱场景中的视觉 grounding 与推理能力。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) often fail under low illumination because their visual grounding is learned predominantly from RGB imagery, whereas thermal infrared preserves complementary scene structure when visible cues degrade. We present Thermo-VL, a wavelength-aware VLM that augments a frozen Molmo-7B backbone with a trainable thermal encoder and a text-guided dual-attention fusion module. Given aligned RGB tokens, thermal tokens, and prompt embeddings, the fusion module conditions thermal features on both language and RGB context, then injects a gated residual into the frozen RGB stream so thermal evidence can be incorporated without disrupting Molmo's pretrained RGB-language interface. We train the model with the standard language-modeling objective together with auxiliary alignment and regularization losses that improve cross-modal grounding and reduce over-reliance on RGB. We also introduce a pixel-aligned RGB-thermal instruction-tuning dataset and Thermo-VL-Bench, a manually screened RGB-thermal VQA benchmark for low-light and cross-spectrum reasoning. Experiments show strong gains on challenging thermal-only and RGB+thermal reasoning tasks, highlighting the value of prompt-conditioned multispectral fusion. Our dataset and code are publicly available at: https://thusharakart.github.io/Thermo-VL

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: RTS包含两项核心设计：其一，使用奖励模型引导噪声优化，将搜索主动导向更有潜力的区域；其二，构建稀疏测试时缩放框架，并结合PCA驱动的曲率分析，在完整去噪空间中优先选择关键中间步骤，从而压缩搜索空间。

Abstract: The efficient Test-Time Scaling (TTS) paradigm offers a promising perspective for enhancing the generation performance of diffusion models. To bridge this gap, we propose RTS, a novel Reward-guided Trajectory Scaling method to fully unlock the generative potential of diffusion models. Unlike existing methods, RTS facilitates the synthesis of refined, high-fidelity images via two core innovations: 1) a reward-guided noise optimization strategy to actively direct the search towards promising regions; and 2) a sparse test-time scaling framework together with a PCA-driven curvature analysis scheme to prioritize key intermediate steps in the entire denoising space, effectively compressing the search space. Experiments show our approach outperforms baselines by 15.6% across GenEval Score, and a 60.4% enhancement in ImageReward score, setting a new SOTA while providing a practical guideline for more effective test-time scaling across diffusion-specific architectures.

### [20] [MAVEN: A Multi-stage Agentic Annotation Pipeline for Video Reasoning Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21917)
*Han Zhang,Wanting Jiang,Tomasz Kornuta,Tian Zheng,Vidya Murali*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MAVEN 是一个多阶段智能体视频事件标注流水线，可将原始视频转化为包含结构化事件描述与 CoT 推理轨迹的多任务训练数据，并支持面向新领域的自动提示词重设计与迭代纠错。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频事件推理模型训练需要大规模、高质量、结构化标注，覆盖事件发生的内容、时间、地点、原因与后果；但人工标注成本高、难以扩展，且跨领域适配需要大量人工提示词工程。

Method: 提出 MAVEN：以指定的 Event of Focus 为核心，先从三种互补字幕层级合成 Multi-Scale Spatio-Temporal Event Description（MSTED），再以 MSTED 作为唯一中间输入生成多任务问答与 CoT。系统还包含智能体驱动的领域适配机制，以及层次化错误分类、根因追踪和定向修改提示词或流水线结构的迭代优化循环。

Result: 在 5,300 多个交通视频上生成标注并微调 Cosmos-Reason2-8B。在私有 CCTV 评测集上，微调模型超过 Gemini 2.5 Pro 和 Gemini 3.1 Flash，相比零样本 MCQ 准确率提升 38.8 个百分点。在 AccidentBench 上，仅用 CCTV 数据训练使 Cosmos-Reason2 提升 10.7 个 MCQ 点并匹配 Gemini 2.5 Pro；加入智能体适配的 dashcam 标注后进一步缩小与 Gemini 3.1 Flash 的差距，RL 后训练后整体超过两个 Gemini 基线。

Conclusion: MAVEN 展示了以结构化中间表示、智能体提示词重构和自动化纠错为核心的视频事件标注范式，可高效生成高质量训练数据，并提升 VLM 在交通及其他监控类视频事件推理任务上的性能与跨域适应能力。

Abstract: Training Vision Language Models (VLMs) for video event reasoning requires high-quality structured annotations capturing not only what happened, but when, where, why, and with what consequence, at a scale manual labelling cannot support. We present MAVEN (Multi-stage Agentic Video Event aNnotation), a multi-stage agentic pipeline that turns raw videos into multi-task training data with Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning traces, organized around a designated Event of Focus. At its core, MAVEN synthesizes a Multi-Scale Spatio-Temporal Event Description (MSTED) from three complementary caption levels; this explicit intermediate serves as the sole input to downstream Q&A generation across multiple task formats. Crucially, MAVEN supports agent-driven domain adaptation: given a new video dataset and target question examples, the agent redesigns all prompts top-down without manual re-engineering. A hierarchical refinement loop further classifies annotation errors against a taxonomy, traces root causes to the originating pipeline stage, and applies targeted edits that rewrite prompts or modify the pipeline structure itself, iteratively improving data quality. We apply MAVEN to label over 5,300 traffic videos and fine-tune Cosmos-Reason2-8B on the resulting data. On a private CCTV evaluation set, fine-tuning surpasses both Gemini 2.5 Pro and 3.1 Flash, including a $+38.8$-point gain in MCQ accuracy over zero-shot. On AccidentBench, CCTV-only training lifts Cosmos-Reason2 by $+10.7$ MCQ points and matches Gemini 2.5 Pro despite seeing no dashcam videos; adding agent-adapted dashcam annotations narrows the gap to Gemini 3.1 Flash, and RL post-training pushes overall performance past both Gemini baselines. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准往往分别评估视觉线索、背景知识、指标估计等能力，难以揭示模型在证据不足或证据整合不完善时，以先验替代真实多模态证据所导致的系统性预测偏差。

Method: 构建包含 50 万个专家参与的多选题和 5 万个回归任务的大规模 SDG 导向视觉语言推理基准 SDGBiasBench；同时提出 CADE（Contrastive Adaptive Debias Ensemble），一种训练-free、即插即用的方法，利用模态特定答案先验进行对比式自适应去偏集成。

Result: 在 SDGBiasBench 上的评测发现当前 VLM 存在内在 SDG 偏差，预测常受 SDG 特定先验驱动而非可靠多模态证据驱动；CADE 在多个 VLM 上显著提升表现，多选准确率最高提升 25%，回归 MAE 最高降低 12 点。

Abstract: Assessing progress toward the Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) requires multi-step reasoning over visual cues, contextual knowledge, and development indicators, where incomplete evidence use and imperfect evidence integration can introduce hidden prediction biases. Real-world SDG monitoring further spans both qualitative judgments and quantitative estimation. However, existing benchmarks typically evaluate these aspects in isolation, obscuring systematic biases that emerge when models substitute priors for evidence. To address this gap, we propose SDGBiasBench, a large-scale benchmark suite for SDG-oriented vision-language reasoning. Spanning 500k expert-involved multiple-choice questions and 50k regression tasks, the benchmark enables comprehensive assessment of both decision-level and estimation-level bias in Vision--Language Models (VLMs). Evaluations on SDGBiasBench reveal an intrinsic SDG bias in current VLMs, where predictions are frequently driven by SDG specific priors rather than reliable multi-modal cues. To mitigate such bias, we propose CADE (Contrastive Adaptive Debias Ensemble), a training-free, plug-and-play method that leverages modality-specific answer priors. CADE yields significant gains on the proposed benchmark, improving multiple-choice accuracy by up to 25% and reducing regression MAE by up to 12 points across multiple VLMs. We hope our work can foster the development of more fair and reliable AI systems for sustainable development.

### [22] [Visual-Advantage On-Policy Distillation for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21924)
*Ruiqi Liu,Xiaolei Lv,Gengsheng Li,Ximo Zhu,Zhiheng Wang,Zhengbo Zhang,Junkai Chen,Zhiheng Li,Bo Li,Jun Gao,Shu Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出 VA-OPD：用教师在有/无细粒度视觉信息时对学生生成序列的打分差异定义“视觉优势”（VA），突出真正承载视觉监督的少量关键 token，从而改进视觉语言模型的在线策略知识蒸馏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准在线策略蒸馏虽能提升学生模型输出质量，但可能没有增强其对视觉输入的依赖；视觉关键信息往往只集中在少量 token 中，若与大量语言脚手架 token 一起平均优化，视觉监督信号会被稀释。

Method: 首先定义 token 级 visual advantage：教师在访问与不访问细粒度视觉细节时，对学生 rollout 的 log-probability 差值。然后提出 VA-OPD，在两个层面使用 VA：按轨迹平均 VA 对 rollout 重加权；在 token 层面将高 VA 与低 VA token 分组，分别计算并平均 KL 蒸馏损失。

Result: 在 Geometry3K 和 ViRL39K 上训练，并在 8 个数学推理与视觉理解基准上评估；基于 Qwen3-VL 系列的 4B、8B、32B 教师模型，VA-OPD 在所有基准上均优于标准在线策略蒸馏，且收益随教师规模和数据规模单调增长。

Conclusion: 视觉语言模型的有效蒸馏需要区分视觉关键信号与普通语言上下文。VA 能识别真正依赖视觉细节的 token，VA-OPD 通过重加权和分组 KL 减少视觉监督稀释，表现出良好的规模扩展趋势。

Abstract: On-policy knowledge distillation has proven effective for language models, yet its application to vision-language models (VLMs) remains underexplored. We observe that standard on-policy distillation can improve a student's output quality while failing to strengthen its reliance on visual input: on vision-critical tokens, the student's predictions remain largely unchanged whether or not fine-grained visual detail is present, even though the teacher's predictions depend heavily on it.To make this difference observable, we introduce visual advantage (VA), the token-level log-probability difference when the teacher scores a student-generated rollout with versus without access to fine-grained visual detail. VA is concentrated in a small minority of tokens, and these high-VA tokens are the ones that actually carry the visual supervision signal. This motivates a distillation objective that treats them differently from language scaffolding, so their contribution is not diluted by the abundant surrounding language tokens.We propose Visual-Advantage On-Policy Distillation (VA-OPD), which uses VA at two granularities: rollout-level reweighting by trajectory-averaged VA, and token-level KL averaged within high-VA and low-VA groups separately. We train on two math datasets (Geometry3K and ViRL39K) and evaluate on eight benchmarks covering both mathematical reasoning and visual understanding, across three teacher sizes (4B, 8B, and 32B) on the Qwen3-VL family. VA-OPD improves over standard on-policy distillation on every benchmark, with the gain growing monotonically along both the teacher-size and data-scale axes, suggesting that these factors compound consistently.

</details>


### [23] [EvoVid: Temporal-Centric Self-Evolution for Video Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21931)
*Shiqi Huang,Ziyue Wang,Zhongrong Zuo,Han Qiu,Qi She,Bihan Wen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EvoVid 提出一种面向视频大语言模型的时间中心自进化框架，使模型能够直接利用未标注原始视频进行强化学习式自我提升，并在多个模型与基准上取得稳定改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Video-LLM 的强化学习训练依赖人工标注任务与答案，成本高且受限于人类专家知识；已有 Questioner-Solver 自博弈自进化方法主要面向文本或图像等静态模态，难以刻画视频推理所需的时间动态。

Method: 提出 EvoVid，通过 Questioner-Solver 自博弈从未标注视频中学习；设计两类时间中心奖励：一是 temporal-aware Questioner reward，通过时间扰动敏感性鼓励生成依赖时间信息的问题；二是 temporal-grounded Solver reward，利用视频片段定位提供自动时间监督。

Result: 在四种基础模型和六个评测基准上的实验显示，EvoVid 相比基础模型和现有自进化基线均带来一致提升，并达到与监督方法具有竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: 时间中心的自进化机制是提升视频理解与推理能力的一种有效且可扩展范式，可减少对人工标注的依赖。

Abstract: Recent Video Large Language Models (Video-LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in video reasoning through reinforcement learning (RL). However, existing RL pipelines rely heavily on human-annotated tasks and solutions, making them costly to scale and fundamentally constrained by human expertise. Self-evolving frameworks have recently emerged as a promising alternative through autonomous Questioner-Solver self-play. Unfortunately, these approaches are primarily designed for static modalities such as text and images, fundamentally failing to capture the temporal dynamics that are central to video reasoning. In this work, we propose $\textbf{EvoVid}$, a temporal-centric self-evolving framework that enables Video-LLMs to improve directly from raw, unannotated videos. Specifically, we introduce two complementary temporal-centric rewards: a temporal-aware Questioner reward that encourages temporally dependent question generation through temporal perturbation sensitivity, and a temporal-grounded Solver reward that provides automatic temporal supervision via inherent video segment localization. Extensive experiments across four base models and six benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over both base models and existing self-evolving baselines, achieving competitive performance with supervised methods. These results highlight temporal-centric self-evolution as an effective and scalable paradigm for video understanding and reasoning.

</details>


### [24] [MLLMs Know When Before Speaking: Revealing and Recovering Temporal Grounding via Attention Cues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21954)
*Dazhao Du,Liao Duan,Jian Liu,Tao Han,Yujia Zhang,Eric Liu,Xi Chen,Song Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文发现多模态大语言模型在视频时间定位中存在“感知—生成”落差：预填充阶段的少数注意力头已能聚焦真实时间区间，但生成答案时注意力会偏移；据此提出无需训练的推理时“读取—再生成”框架，显著提升多个模型在VTG基准上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频时间定位要求模型根据文本查询在未裁剪视频中定位事件起止时间，是检验MLLM是否理解“何时发生”的关键任务。现有MLLM虽能流畅描述视频，但时间戳预测不可靠；已有改进方法要么依赖昂贵的时间标注后训练，要么采用粗糙的免训练启发式方法，因此需要一种低成本且更精确的推理时改进方案。

Method: 作者分析MLLM的跨模态注意力，发现预填充阶段存在稀疏的Temporal Grounding Heads（TG-Heads），其查询到视频的注意力集中在真实事件区间。基于此，方法先将TG-Head的预填充注意力转化为去偏的帧级相关性信号，提取高注意力时间区间；随后重新调用MLLM，并通过视频裁剪或注意力掩码将视觉上下文限制在该区间，以抑制无关视觉干扰。整个框架不更新参数，也不改变模型结构。

Result: 该方法在MiMo-VL-7B、Qwen3-VL-8B和TimeLens-8B上，以及三个视频时间定位基准中均带来稳定提升，最高提升达到+3.5 mIoU。

Conclusion: 研究表明，MLLM在生成最终答案前往往已经通过内部注意力捕获了目标时间区间，但生成过程会丢失或偏移该信号。利用预填充阶段TG-Heads的注意力进行区间读取并重新生成答案，是一种有效、训练无关、架构无关的视频时间定位增强策略。

Abstract: Video temporal grounding (VTG), which localizes the start and end times of a queried event in an untrimmed video, is a key test of whether multimodal large language models (MLLMs) understand not only what happens but also when it happens. Although modern MLLMs describe video content fluently, their timestamp predictions remain unreliable, while existing remedies either require costly post-training on temporal annotations or rely on coarse training-free heuristics. In this work, we probe the cross-modal attention of MLLMs and uncover a perception-generation gap. Our key finding is that MLLMs often know the target interval during prefill, but lose this signal when generating the final answer. In the prefill stage, a sparse set of attention heads, which we call \emph{Temporal Grounding Heads} (TG-Heads), concentrates query-to-video attention on the ground-truth interval. During autoregressive decoding, however, the answer tokens shift attention away from this interval toward visually salient but query-irrelevant segments. This observation motivates an inference-time read-then-regenerate framework. We first convert TG-Head prefill attention into a debiased frame-level relevance signal and extract the high-attention interval it highlights. We then re-invoke the MLLM with visual context restricted to this interval, using video cropping or attention masking to suppress distractors. Without parameter updates and architectural changes, our framework consistently improves MiMo-VL-7B, Qwen3-VL-8B, and TimeLens-8B on three VTG benchmarks, with gains of up to +3.5 mIoU. The project website can be found at https://ddz16.github.io/mllmsknowwhen.github.io/.

</details>


### [25] [Bounding-Box Trajectories Matter for Video Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21957)
*Inpyo Song,Jangwon Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 TrajVAD，将人体/目标边界框轨迹作为视频异常检测的核心线索，并用归一化流建模正常运动轨迹；实验显示仅轨迹版本已优于多种姿态方法，结合姿态后性能进一步提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频异常检测受外观、视角和场景动态变化影响较大。现有姿态方法虽对外观变化鲁棒、能紧凑描述人体运动，但通常忽视了姿态流程中天然可获得的边界框轨迹信息。作者认为轨迹可直接反映运动学模式，是一种有效但未充分利用的异常检测模态。

Method: 提出 TrajVAD 框架，显式利用多类别边界框轨迹作为异常线索，并采用 normalizing flows 学习正常轨迹的概率分布/运动学规律。TrajVAD-T 为仅使用轨迹的版本，不需要姿态估计；TrajVAD-P 在轨迹基础上进一步融合姿态信息。

Conclusion: 边界框轨迹是视频异常检测中有效且被低估的模态。相比单纯依赖姿态，轨迹建模能提供强异常判别能力；与姿态融合后可进一步提升检测性能。

Abstract: Video anomaly detection is critical for public safety and security, yet remains highly challenging despite extensive research due to large variations in appearance, viewpoint, and scene dynamics. Among existing approaches, human pose-based methods have emerged as a major line of research, showing strong performance since many anomalies in public datasets involve humans and pose representations are robust to appearance changes while providing compact motion descriptions. However, these methods often overlook bounding-box trajectories, although such information is inherently available in pose-based pipelines. In this paper, we explicitly leverage these trajectories as a primary anomaly cue. We present TrajVAD, a framework that models multi-class bounding-box trajectories using normalizing flows to learn normal kinematic patterns. Its trajectory-only variant (TrajVAD-T) eliminates pose estimation and surpasses all compared pose-based methods on ShanghaiTech in AP (87.7%), while achieving the best results on MSAD. An extended version (TrajVAD-P) incorporates pose information and further improves performance to 88.6% AUROC and 90.9% AP on ShanghaiTech, highlighting bounding-box trajectories as an effective yet underexplored modality for video anomaly detection.

### [26] [Foresee-to-Ground: From Predictive Temporal Perception to Evidence-Driven Reasoning for Video Temporal Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21973)
*Zelin Zheng,Xinyan Liu,Ruixin Li,Antoni B. Chan,Guorong Li,Qingming Huang,Laiyun Qing*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 Foresee-to-Ground（F2G），将视频时间定位从直接生成时间戳改造为可验证的“先识别、再测量”流程，以提升边界预测稳定性与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Video-LLM 在视频时间定位（VTG）中通常从非结构化视觉 token 流直接生成时间戳，容易出现数值不稳定、边界不一致、预测难以验证等问题。

Method: F2G 结合预测式时间感知与证据驱动推理：学习边界敏感的时间表示，构建覆盖全视频的候选事件片段证据池，并将这些片段作为可引用证据单元提供给 LLM，使边界预测与显式事件假设绑定；同时将事件识别与精确边界测量解耦。

Result: 大量实验表明，F2G 在多种基准上持续提升时间定位精度，可稳健迁移到不同 Video-LLM 骨干，并保持通用视频理解能力。

Conclusion: F2G 通过结构化证据与识别-测量解耦机制，提高了视频时间定位的准确性、稳定性与可验证性，是对直接时间戳生成范式的有效改进。

Abstract: Current Video-LLM approaches for Video Temporal Grounding (VTG) typically rely on direct timestamp generation from an unstructured visual-token stream, often leading to brittle numerics and inconsistent boundaries. To address this, we propose Foresee-to-Ground (F2G), a framework that reformulates VTG as a verifiable Identify-then-Measure problem. F2G integrates Predictive Temporal Perception with Evidence-Driven Reasoning: it learns boundary-sensitive temporal representations to build a video-wide evidence pool of candidate event segments, and exposes these segments to the LLM as citable evidence units that bind boundary prediction to explicit event hypotheses. By decoupling event identification from precise boundary measurement, F2G stabilizes grounding and makes predictions verifiable. Extensive experiments demonstrate that F2G consistently improves grounding accuracy across diverse benchmarks, transfers robustly across different Video-LLM backbones, and preserves general video understanding capabilities.

### [27] [Video as Natural Augmentation: Towards Unified AI-Generated Image and Video Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21977)

TL;DR: 本文指出现有AI生成图像检测器在视频帧场景下容易失效，并提出VINA框架，通过联合训练图像与视频帧、引入跨模态监督对比学习，提高AIGC检测的跨源、跨流程、跨模态泛化能力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者系统分析失效原因，发现跨模态差距来自两类因素：一是与生成模型无关的视频处理偏移，如颜色转换、编码压缩、缩放和模糊；二是现代视频生成器引入的模型特异性指纹。基于此提出VINA，将视频帧作为物理真实的自然增强，与图像数据联合训练，并使用跨模态监督对比目标对齐图像与视频表示，使其共享真实/伪造判别边界。

Result: 在14个图像、视频和真实场景基准上，VINA在多数评测设置中达到最优性能，带来图像到视频与视频到图像的双向提升，并改善鲁棒性和迁移能力。

Conclusion: 视频帧可作为有效的自然增强信号，帮助弥合AI生成内容检测中的图像—视频模态鸿沟；联合图像/视频训练与跨模态表示对齐能够显著提升检测器的泛化能力，无需复杂增强或针对特定数据集调参。

Abstract: AI-generated content (AIGC) is rapidly improving, creating an urgent need for detectors that generalize across data sources, deployment pipelines, and visual modalities. A strongly generalizable detector should remain robust under distributional variations. However, we identify a consistent failure mode: SOTA AI-generated image detectors often collapse when applied to frames extracted from videos. Through systematic analysis, we show that this cross-modal gap arises from both entangled synthesis-agnostic video processing shifts, including color conversion, codec compression, resizing, and blur, and model-specific fingerprints introduced by modern video generators. Motivated by these findings, we propose VINA (Video as Natural Augmentation), a unified AIGC detection framework that jointly trains on image and video data. VINA uses video frames as physically grounded natural augmentations and further introduces a cross-modal supervised contrastive objective to align image and video representations under a shared real/fake decision boundary. Extensive experiments on 14 image, video, and in-the-wild benchmarks show that VINA delivers bidirectional gains, improves robustness and transferability, and achieves state-of-the-art performance across nearly all evaluated settings without complex augmentation or dataset-specific tuning.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) represent a significant leap towards empathetic agents, demonstrating remarkable capabilities in emotion understanding. In this paper, we bridge this gap by introducing a steering-vector-based causal attribution framework tailored for descriptive emotional reasoning. To this end, we construct a specialized dataset to demystify the emotional circuits underlying the three-stage ``Adapt-Aggregate-Execute'' mechanism. Crucially, we discover a functional decoupling: visual emotional cues are aggregated in middle layers via sentiment-specific attention heads, but are subsequently translated into narrative generation in deep layers through emotion-general pathways. Guided by these insights, we regulate the emotional information routing to strengthen attention flow and amplify the semantic activation to consolidate expression. Extensive experiments on the comprehensive MER-UniBench demonstrate that our methods significantly improve performance via inference-time intervention, effectively mitigating emotional hallucinations and corroborating the causal fidelity of the discovered circuits.

### [29] [RiT: Vanilla Diffusion Transformers Suffice in Representation Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21981)
*Le Zhang,Ning Mang,Aishwarya Agrawal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出在冻结的 DINOv2 表征空间中进行基于 x-prediction 的 flow matching，构建 RiT，在 ImageNet 256×256 上取得优于强基线的生成质量与采样效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，在像素空间中回归干净数据点的 x-prediction 能利用低维流形结构；作者进一步追问：预训练表征空间是否在相近内在维度下，具有更利于 flow matching 学习的分布几何性质。

Method: 作者比较像素空间、SD-VAE 潜空间和 DINOv2 特征空间的几何统计特性，并基于冻结 DINOv2 特征训练一个 vanilla Diffusion Transformer，即 Representation Image Transformer（RiT）。模型采用 x-prediction、维度感知噪声调度，以及联合 [CLS]-patch 建模。

Result: DINOv2 与像素空间内在维度接近（约 33），但有效秩高 7.3 倍、协方差条件数好 35 倍、过量峰度低 11.5 倍、流形内插误差低 1.7 倍。RiT 在 ImageNet 256×256 上无引导 FID 1.45，有 classifier-free guidance 时 FID 1.14，并以 676M 参数优于 839M 参数的 DiT^DH-XL。采样方面，5 个 Heun 步达到 FID 2.0，10 步达到 1.25。

Conclusion: 预训练表征空间，尤其是 DINOv2 特征，不仅保留低维流形结构，还提供更均匀、条件更好的分布几何，从而使 flow-matching 回归更稳定高效，并可用更简单的 Transformer 架构实现高质量、低步数图像生成。

Abstract: Flow matching with $x$-prediction -- regressing the clean data point rather than the ambient velocity -- is known to exploit low-dimensional manifold structure effectively in pixel space \cite{li2025back}. We ask whether a pretrained representation space, while containing a low-dimensional data manifold of comparable intrinsic dimensionality, offers a distribution more favorable for flow-matching learning. Comparing pixel, SD-VAE, and DINOv2 features along four geometric axes, we find that pixel and DINOv2 share nearly identical intrinsic dimensionalities (both $\hat{d}\!\approx\!33$) yet DINOv2 exhibits $7.3\times$ higher effective rank, $35\times$ better covariance conditioning, $11.5\times$ lower excess kurtosis, and $1.7\times$ lower on-manifold interpolation error; SD-VAE latents are consistently intermediate, indicating that the advantage stems from representation-learning objectives rather than mere compression. These statistical properties render the flow-matching regression well-conditioned and remove the need for the specialized prediction heads or Riemannian transport used by prior DINOv2 diffusion methods. We propose the \emph{Representation Image Transformer} (RiT): a vanilla Diffusion Transformer trained by $x$-prediction on frozen DINOv2 features, augmented only by a dimension-aware noise schedule and joint \texttt{[CLS]}-patch modeling. On ImageNet $256{\times}256$, RiT attains FID 1.45 without guidance and 1.14 with classifier-free guidance, outperforming DiT$^\text{DH}$-XL with $19\%$ fewer parameters (676M vs.\ 839M). The resulting ODE is efficiently solvable at coarse discretizations: with classifier-free guidance, $5$ Heun steps already reach FID 2.0 and $10$ steps reach 1.25, without distillation or consistency training. Code at https://github.com/lezhang7/RiT.

</details>


### [30] [Learning Spatiotemporal Sensitivity in Video LLMs via Counterfactual Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21988)
*Dazhao Du,Jian Liu,Jialong Qin,Tao Han,Bohai Gu,Fangqi Zhu,Yujia Zhang,Eric Liu,Xi Chen,Song Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出 CRPO，一种面向视频大语言模型的双分支强化学习框架，通过反事实视频与跨分支奖励提升模型对时空动态变化的敏感性，并在新基准 DyBench 上取得明显提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Video LLM 虽然在常规基准上表现较好，但常依赖单帧线索或语言先验等捷径回答问题，而不是实际建模视频中的时空动态。强化学习后训练若只使用答案正确性奖励，可能进一步强化这些捷径策略。因此，作者希望通过反事实视角约束模型：当视觉世界改变而问题不变时，答案是否应随之改变。

Method: 作者提出 Counterfactual Relational Policy Optimization（CRPO）。该方法构造水平翻转、时间反转等反事实视频，并在原始视频分支和反事实视频分支上共同训练；同时设计 Counterfactual Relation Reward（CRR），根据问题类型约束两分支答案关系：动态问题要求答案随反事实变化而改变，静态问题要求答案保持一致。作者还构建 DyBench，一个成对反事实视频基准，覆盖可逆动态、运动方向和事件顺序，并采用严格的 pair-accuracy 指标抑制固定答案捷径。

Result: 实验表明，CRPO 在时空敏感性评测上优于已有强化学习方法，同时保持有竞争力的通用视频理解能力。在 Qwen3-VL-8B 上，CRPO 相比基础模型使 DyBench P-Acc 提升 7.7，TimeBlind I-Acc 提升 8.2。

Conclusion: CRPO 通过反事实双分支训练和答案关系奖励，有效降低了视频模型对静态捷径和语言先验的依赖，提升了其对视频时空动态的真实感知与推理能力。

Abstract: Video large language models (Video LLMs) achieve strong benchmark accuracy, yet often answer video questions through shortcuts such as single-frame cues and language priors rather than by tracking spatiotemporal dynamics. This issue is exacerbated in RL post-training, where correctness-only rewards can further reinforce shortcut policies that obtain high reward without tracking video dynamics. We address this by asking a controlled counterfactual question: if the visual world changed while the question remained fixed, should the answer change or stay the same? Based on this view, we propose \textbf{Counterfactual Relational Policy Optimization (CRPO)}, a dual-branch RL framework for improving \emph{spatiotemporal sensitivity}. CRPO constructs counterfactual videos through horizontal flips and temporal reversals, trains on both original and counterfactual branches, and introduces a \textbf{Counterfactual Relation Reward (CRR)} between their answers. CRR encourages answers to change for dynamic questions and remain unchanged for static questions. This cross-branch constraint makes it difficult for shortcut policies to be consistently rewarded across both branches. To evaluate this property, we introduce \textbf{DyBench}, a paired counterfactual video benchmark with 3,014 videos covering reversible dynamics, moving direction, and event sequence, together with a strict pair-accuracy metric that prevents fixed-answer shortcuts from inflating scores. Experiments show that CRPO outperforms prior RL methods on spatiotemporal-sensitive evaluations while maintaining competitive general video performance. On Qwen3-VL-8B, CRPO improves DyBench P-Acc by +7.7 and TimeBlind I-Acc by +8.2 over the base model, indicating improved spatiotemporal sensitivity rather than stronger reliance on static shortcuts. The project website can be found at https://ddz16.github.io/crpo.github.io/ .

</details>

Conclusion: HistoBIT3D 与所提出的虚拟染色方法建立了一个可量化验证、结构保真且可扩展的三维虚拟 H&E 染色流程，推动了无需玻片制备的三维计算病理学发展。

Back-illumination Interference Tomography (BIT) is a new phase microscopy technology that provides rapid, non-destructive volumetric imaging of unprocessed tissues. However, translating BIT volumes into clinically interpretable H&E images remains challenging, particularly due to shift-variant contrast and the absence of quantitative validation benchmarks. We introduce HistoBIT3D, the first voxel-wise paired BIT and fluorescence-labeled nuclei dataset, enabling quantitative evaluation of structural preservation in unsupervised virtual staining against ground-truth nuclear distributions. Using this dataset, we present a novel virtual staining framework that translates BIT volumes with shift-variant contrast into realistic H&E volumes by leveraging bidirectional multiscale content consistency and cross-domain style reuse to enhance structural fidelity and perceptual realism. Our method achieves state-of-the-art realism metrics while significantly improving 3D nuclei segmentation accuracy and boundary preservation under zero-shot Cellpose evaluation. Together, these contributions establish a quantitatively validated, structurally faithful, and scalable pipeline for 3D virtual H&E staining, advancing the paradigm of slide-free, volumetric computational histopathology. Our data and code are available at: https://github.com/aasong113/HistoBIT3D_VirtualStaining.

### [32] [Rethinking Token Reduction for Diffusion Models via Output-Similarity-Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22011)
*Hangyeol Lee,Hyojeong Lee,Joo-Young Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DiTo提出面向输出相似性的Diffusion Transformer令牌减少范式，通过复用相邻时间步的输出令牌匹配关系，在相近加速下显著提升恢复质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DiT令牌减少方法主要沿用ViT中的输入令牌相似性准则，忽略生成模型的核心目标是最小化输出恢复误差，因此与生成任务中应关注输出令牌相似性的目标存在错配。

Method: 作者提出DiTo：利用相邻扩散时间步之间输出令牌相似性稳定保持的观察，在Matching时间步建立令牌对应关系，并在后续多个Reduction时间步复用；进一步提出PMR引导的区间调度以确定匹配频率，并提出频率感知令牌匹配，通过选择频率惩罚缓解重复复用导致的局部误差和块状伪影。

Result: 大量实验表明，在相近加速比下，DiTo相比已有令牌减少方法获得1.6–3.9 dB的PSNR提升，并形成更优的速度-质量Pareto前沿。

Conclusion: DiTo证明了在DiT加速中，面向输出的令牌减少比仅依赖输入相似性更契合生成模型目标，可在保持生成质量的同时实现有效计算削减。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) achieve superior image generation quality but suffer from quadratic computational complexity relative to token count. While various token reduction (TR) methods have been proposed to mitigate this cost, they overlook the primary objective of generative models: minimizing recovery error, which requires reflecting output token similarity. They rely solely on input token similarity inherited from reduction-only ViT paradigms, leading to a fundamental misalignment with this objective.
  To bridge this gap, we propose DiTo, a novel TR paradigm that shifts the focus toward output-centric token reduction. Based on the observation that output token similarity is consistently preserved across adjacent timesteps, DiTo utilizes prior-step similarities as an effective proxy to establish token correspondences at a Matching timestep, which are then reused across multiple subsequent Reduction timesteps. To optimize this interleaved scheduling, we propose Pair Match Ratio (PMR)-guided Interval Scheduling to determine the optimal matching frequency. Furthermore, to mitigate localized approximation errors and resulting blocking artifacts caused by repeated reuse, we propose Frequency-aware Token Matching by incorporating a selection-frequency penalty. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DiTo consistently outperforms existing TR methods with 1.6-3.9 dB higher PSNR at comparable speedups, achieving a superior Pareto frontier.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3D点云数据结构不规则，现有3D多模态模型缺乏显式推理能力；尽管CoT在大语言模型和图像多模态模型中有效，但在3D点云理解中的应用仍不足。

Method: 提出数据中心的两阶段流程：首先利用视觉语言模型进行质量评估与参考引导的数据精炼，提升点云-文本指令数据质量；随后通过Human-in-the-Loop Prompt Optimization（HiLPO）合成高质量推理路径。基于此构建含55K样本的PoCoTI数据集，并用其微调PointLLM得到PointLLM-R。

Abstract: Understanding 3D point clouds through language remains a fundamental challenge in computer graphics and visual computing, due to the irregular structure of point cloud data and the lack of explicit reasoning in existing 3D multimodal models. In this paper, we propose a data-centric framework for constructing large-scale CoT supervision tailored to 3D point cloud understanding. Our framework consists of a two-stage pipeline that first refines point-text instruction data via vision-language-model-based quality evaluation and reference-guided refinement, and then synthesizes high-quality reasoning paths through Human-in-the-Loop Prompt Optimization (HiLPO). Using this approach, we build PoCoTI, a CoT-enhanced point-text instruction-following dataset containing 55K samples with explicit reasoning paths. Fine-tuning PointLLM on PoCoTI yields PointLLM-R, a reasoning-capable 3D multimodal language model. Extensive experiments on generative 3D classification and captioning demonstrate that PointLLM-R achieves state-of-the-art performance and generalizes robustly to real-world scanned point clouds and multi-turn dialogue scenarios.

### [34] [ORBIS: Output-Guided Token Reduction with Distribution-Aware Matching for Video Diffusion Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22015)
*Hangyeol Lee,Joo-Young Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ORBIS 是面向视频 Diffusion Transformer 的软硬件协同加速器，通过更准确的 token 相似度估计与分布感知匹配算法提升 token 削减比例，并用专用流水线硬件隐藏匹配开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频 DiT 中 3D 时空注意力会随帧数增加显著拉长 token 序列，导致计算成本急剧上升。现有 token reduction 方法虽利用空间冗余降低开销，但相似度估计不准确、匹配算法过于轻量，造成匹配质量差、加速收益有限。

Method: 提出 ORBIS：利用前一扩散 timestep 的输出激活来估计更准确的 token 间相似度；设计 Distribution-Aware Token Matching（DATM）算法，建模全局 token 分布并显式最小化 token-pair loss；进一步通过专用深度流水线硬件完全隐藏 DATM 延迟，并采用量化降低硬件成本。

Result: 实验显示，相比现有方法 AsymRnR，ORBIS 获得约 2 倍更高的 token reduction ratio；相比 NVIDIA A100 GPU，最高实现 4.5 倍加速和 79.3% 能耗降低。DATM 硬件仅占总面积 2.4%，且精度损失可忽略。

Conclusion: ORBIS 通过算法与硬件协同设计解决视频 DiT token reduction 中匹配质量与运行开销的矛盾，在保持生成质量的同时显著提升推理效率与能效，适合高成本视频生成模型加速。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformer (DiT) has emerged as a powerful model architecture for generating high-quality images and videos. In the case of video DiT, 3D Spatio-Temporal Attention increases token length in proportion to the number of frames, sharply increasing computational cost. Token reduction methods mitigate this cost by exploiting spatial redundancy, but existing approaches rely on inaccurate similarity estimates and lightweight matching algorithms, resulting in poor matching quality and only marginal acceleration.
  To overcome these limitations, we propose ORBIS, an SW-HW co-designed accelerator for video DiT. ORBIS leverages the output activation from the previous timestep to obtain more accurate inter-token similarity, substantially improving matching quality and enabling a higher token reduction ratio. We further introduce a Distribution-Aware Token Matching (DATM) algorithm that captures global token distribution and explicitly minimizes token-pair loss for additional gains. To fully hide DATM latency, we design specialized, deeply pipelined hardware and minimize its hardware cost through quantization, occupying only 2.4% of total area with negligible accuracy loss. Extensive experiments show that ORBIS achieves about 2x higher token reduction ratio than the state-of-the-art approach, AsymRnR, while delivering up to 4.5x speedup and 79.3% energy reduction compared to an NVIDIA A100 GPU.

### [37] [ForeSplat: Optimization-Aware Foresight for Feed-Forward 3D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22020)
*Yuke Li,Weihang Liu,Cheng Zhang,Yuefeng Zhang,Jiadi Cui,Zixuan Wang,Junran Ding,Haoyu Wu,Yujiao Shi,Jingyi Yu,Xin Lou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ForeSplat通过优化感知训练，让前馈3D Gaussian Splatting模型输出更适合后续快速优化的初始化，从而用更少 refinement 步数获得更高重建质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前馈3DGS虽能快速单次重建，但受限于大规模3D标注稀缺，难以达到逐场景优化的质量；现有训练只关注零步渲染误差，未考虑预测结果是否适合作为下游优化器的良好初始化。

Method: 提出ForeSplat框架，将部分建模压力交给后续优化器，并通过MetaGrad进行优化感知微调。MetaGrad展开短程内循环优化轨迹，采样多个锚点状态，聚合一阶梯度作为替代的优化感知信号回传到预测头，避免对3DGS优化器进行昂贵的高阶求导；推理阶段不增加额外成本。

Result: 在AnySplat、Pi3X以及面向边缘部署的蒸馏变体等不同骨干上，ForeSplat训练得到的初始化均能以更少 refinement 步数收敛，并达到高于原始模型的峰值重建质量，甚至优于原始模型充分优化后的结果。

Conclusion: ForeSplat有效弥合了摊销式前馈预测与逐场景优化之间的差距，为轻量化、高保真、秒级3D重建提供了实用途径。

Abstract: Feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) models offer fast single-pass reconstruction,but scaling them to match per-scene optimization quality is fundamentally hindered by the scarcity of large-scale 3D annotations.A practical compromise is predict-then-refine,where post-prediction optimization compensates for the limited capacity of the feed-forward network.However,standard feed-forward 3DGS is trained solely for zero-step rendering error,ignoring whether its output constitutes a good initialization for the downstream optimizer.We present ForeSplat,an optimization-aware training framework that equips feed-forward 3DGS models to produce initializations explicitly designed for rapid,effective refinement.By offloading part of the scene-modeling burden to the optimizer,ForeSplat substantially reduces the capacity pressure on the feed-forward model,making high-quality reconstruction feasible even with compact networks.At its core is MetaGrad,a lightweight multi-anchor meta-gradient training rule that bypasses costly higher-order differentiation through the 3DGS optimizer.MetaGrad unrolls a short inner-loop refinement trajectory,samples anchor states,and back-propagates aggregated first-order gradients to the prediction head as a surrogate optimization-aware signal.This fine-tuning adds no inference cost and enables high-quality reconstruction within seconds after a few refinement steps.We instantiate ForeSplat on diverse backbones,including AnySplat,Pi3X,and a distilled variant tailored for edge deployment.Across all tested architectures,a ForeSplat-trained initialization converges in fewer refinement steps and reaches a higher peak reconstruction quality than its vanilla counterpart,even fully converged.The framework consistently bridges the gap between amortized prediction and per-scene optimization,establishing a practical path toward lightweight,high-fidelity 3D reconstruction.

### [38] [SO-Mamba: State-Ownership Mamba for Unrolled MRI Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22031)
*Pengcheng Fang,Hongli Chen,Fangfang Tang,Feng Liu,Xiaohao Cai,Shanshan Shan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 SO-Mamba，用于加速 MRI 重建中的展开式求解器，通过区分 Mamba 阶段内证据的“状态归属”来提升长程结构一致性与重建质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 加速 MRI 重建需要在缺失采样条件下恢复细节并保持大范围解剖结构一致。Mamba 等状态空间模型适合高效长程建模，但在与数据一致性耦合的展开式重建中，不同阶段对应不同重建迭代；若将跨阶段应持续保留的驻留内容与依赖当前更新的非驻留证据混入同一递归路径，可能导致状态污染与信息角色混淆。

Method: 作者提出 State-Ownership Mamba regularizer（SO-Mamba）。其核心为 State-Ownership Router（SOR），将每个 Mamba 阶段中的重建证据划分为三类：递归驻留载体、状态接口访问证据、非状态输出校正。驻留载体进入 Mamba 内容递归路径；非驻留证据不进入递归内容路由，而是用于 B/C 状态接口的仿射调制，并通过输出校正通道贡献结果。此外，提出两级 outer-band leakage 诊断，分别度量 selective-scan 状态轨迹与 post-scan Mamba 读出中的外带能量，以区分隐藏状态存储与读出表达。

Result: 在五个公开 MRI 重建基准上进行实验，覆盖不同解剖部位、采样模式与线圈配置。结果显示 SO-Mamba 相比 CNN、Transformer 和 Mamba 类基线均取得稳定性能提升，同时保持有竞争力的计算效率。

Conclusion: SO-Mamba 通过显式建模状态归属，避免将持久性重建内容与阶段依赖更新证据混合到同一递归路径，从而改善展开式 MRI 重建中的结构一致性、细节恢复和泛化表现。

Abstract: Accelerated MRI reconstruction requires recovering missing details while preserving anatomically coherent structures across large spatial regions. State-space models such as Mamba provide efficient long-range modeling, making them attractive learned regularizers for unrolled reconstruction. However, in a data-consistency-coupled unrolled solver, different stages operate on different reconstruction iterates, where the resident carrier should preserve coherent reconstruction content across stages while stage-dependent non-resident evidence is tied to the current update. Treating these roles uniformly can place persistent resident-carrier evidence and update-dependent non-resident evidence into the same recurrent content route. We therefore propose SO-Mamba, a state-ownership Mamba regularizer that assigns reconstruction evidence within each Mamba stage to recurrent residency, state-interface access, and non-state output correction. SO-Mamba implements this ownership rule with a State-Ownership Router (SOR), which constructs a resident carrier for recurrent content and routes non-resident evidence to affine modulation of the B/C state interfaces and an output correction outlet. The resident carrier supplies the Mamba content route, while the non-resident evidence stream adapts the state interfaces and contributes through the output outlet without entering the recurrent content route. We further introduce a two-level outer-band leakage diagnostic that separates hidden-state storage from readout expression by measuring outer-band energy in the selective-scan state trajectory and the post-scan Mamba readout. Experiments on five public MRI reconstruction benchmarks spanning diverse anatomies, sampling patterns, and coil configurations show that SO-Mamba consistently improves over CNN-, Transformer-, and Mamba-based baselines with competitive computational efficiency.

</details>


### [39] [AgroVG: A Large-Scale Multi-Source Benchmark for Agricultural Visual Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22034)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: AgroVG 揭示了现有视觉语言与视觉定位模型在农业复杂场景中的显著短板，尤其是在多实例集合预测、高精度掩码定位和目标不存在时的可靠拒答方面。该基准可作为推动农业 AI 视觉定位能力提升的重要评测平台。

Abstract: Visual grounding, the task of localizing objects described by natural-language expressions, is a foundational capability for agricultural AI systems, enabling applications such as selective weeding, disease monitoring, and targeted harvesting. Reliable evaluation of agricultural visual grounding remains challenging because agricultural targets are often small, repetitive, occluded, or irregularly shaped, and instructions may refer to one, many, or no objects in an image. Evaluating this capability therefore requires jointly testing localization accuracy, target-set completeness, and existence-aware abstention. To address these challenges, we introduce \textbf{AgroVG}, a multi-source benchmark that formulates agricultural grounding as generalized set prediction: given an image and a referring expression, a model must return all matching target instances or abstain when no target is present. AgroVG contains 10{,}071 annotation-grounded image-query pairs from ten source datasets across six target families: crop/weed, fruit, wheat head, pest, plant disease, and tree canopy. It supports bounding-box grounding (T1) across all six families and instance-mask grounding (T2) on sources with reliable instance-level pixel annotations, with queries covering single-target, multi-target, and target-absent regimes. AgroVG further provides task-specific protocols for box-set matching and query-level mask coverage. Zero-shot evaluation of 26 model configurations spanning closed-source MLLMs, open-source VLMs, and specialized grounding systems reveals persistent gaps: the best multi-target Set-$F_1$ reaches only 0.35, and the best positive-query mask success rate at IoU@0.75 remains below 0.17. Data and code are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/AgroVG-5172/ .

### [40] [GA-VLN: Geometry-Aware BEV Representation for Efficient Vision-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22036)
*Jiahao Yang,Zihan Wang,Xiangyang Li,Xing Zhu,Yujun Shen,Yinghao Xu,Shuqiang Jiang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GA-BEV/GA-VLN：将RGB-D视觉特征投影到3D并聚合为以智能体为中心的BEV空间表示，同时融合预训练3D基础模型特征，以更少token提升VLN效率与空间推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言导航方法依赖密集RGB视频输入，产生大量patch token，计算开销高；同时缺少显式空间结构，限制了几何理解与空间推理能力。

Method: 构建Geometry-Aware BEV表示：首先利用RGB-D输入将视觉特征投影到3D空间，并聚合成保持几何一致性的agent-centric BEV地图；其次将预训练3D基础模型的特征注入BEV空间，引入来自大规模3D重建任务的隐式结构先验；最后将该紧凑3D-grounded表示接入基于MLLM的导航系统。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在仅使用导航数据的条件下达到当前最优结果，不依赖DAgger数据增强或混合VQA训练，同时显著降低token冗余并提升导航效率与性能。

Conclusion: GA-BEV通过结合显式深度投影与隐式3D结构先验，提供了紧凑且空间表达能力强的导航表示，证明了几何感知BEV表征在提升VLN模型数据效率、计算效率和空间推理能力方面的有效性。

Abstract: Despite significant progress in Vision-Language Navigation (VLN), existing approaches still rely on dense RGB videos that produce excessive patch tokens and lack explicit spatial structure, resulting in substantial computational overhead and limited spatial reasoning. To address these issues, we introduce the Geometry-Aware BEV (GA-BEV) - a compact, 3D-grounded feature representation that integrates both explicit and implicit geometric cues into multimodal large language model (MLLM) - based navigation systems. We construct BEV spatial maps from RGB-D inputs by projecting visual features into 3D space and aggregating them into an agent-centric layout that preserves geometric consistency while reducing token redundancy. To further enrich geometric understanding, we incorporate features from a pretrained 3D foundation model into the BEV space, injecting structural priors learned from large-scale 3D reconstruction tasks. Together, these complementary cues - explicit depth-based projection and implicit learned priors - yield compact yet spatially expressive representations that substantially improve navigation efficiency and performance. Experiments show that our method achieves state-of-the-art results using only navigation data, without DAgger augmentation or mixed VQA training, demonstrating the robustness and data efficiency of the proposed GA-VLN framework.

Abstract: Accurate localization of myocardial infarction is essential for risk stratification. While LGE-MRI remains the gold standard, it is resource-intensive. Integrating cine MRI with ECG enables a more detailed representation of infarct properties. Existing inverse MI inference methods overlook realistic scar morphology and cardiac repolarization, reducing sensitivity to subtle ECG variations and interpretability of infarct-induced electrophysiological changes. In this paper, we propose a novel framework for noninvasive MI localization using cardiac digital twins. To bridge the domain gap between simulation and reality, we introduce an anatomy-aware stochastic infarct synthesis strategy to synthesize realistic, irregular scars with border zones, mimicking ischemic transmural progression. We then construct a virtual cohort to simulate QRS-T waveforms, capturing both depolarization and repolarization dynamics. Furthermore, we design a Physiology and Anatomy Aware Network (PAA-Net) that jointly encodes 3D myocardial geometry and multi-lead ECGs to infer infarct areas with varying localizations, sizes, spatial extents, and transmuralities. Experimental results demonstrate that our framework significantly outperforms existing methods in inverse inference, achieving Dice scores of 0.7391 and 0.5503 for scar and border zone segmentation, respectively, while further enhancing the interpretability of the ECG-infarct relationship. ### [42] [Broken Memories: Detecting and Mitigating Memorization in Diffusion Models with Degraded Generations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22050)
*Yuanmin Huang,Mi Zhang,Chen Chen,Feifei Li,Geng Hong,Xiaoyu You,Min Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文发现扩散模型记忆训练数据会引发生成过程中的内部数值不稳定，并提出基于潜变量更新范数的在线检测与自适应缓解框架，在不改动提示词或引导策略的情况下抑制记忆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型虽能生成高质量图像，但可能记忆训练样本，带来隐私与版权风险。已有方法往往难以在保持语义一致性和图像质量的同时，高效识别并缓解记忆现象，因此需要一种在线、低开销且不干扰生成条件的解决方案。

Method: 作者从数值方法稳定性分析获得启发，提出“经验稳定区域”，利用生成过程中每一步潜变量更新范数来刻画稳定/不稳定行为；在此基础上构建逐步检测机制，并在发现不稳定迹象时进行自适应缓解，以抑制由记忆导致的异常生成。

Result: 在 Stable Diffusion 1.4 上的实验显示，该方法检测性能 AUC 超过 0.999，缓解后记忆率降至 0.0%，且额外计算开销极低，约每张图像 0.01 秒。

Conclusion: 论文表明，训练数据记忆可通过生成过程中的数值不稳定信号被有效识别；基于稳定性区域的在线检测与缓解框架能够高精度、低开销地降低记忆风险，同时基本保持语义保真度和图像质量。

Abstract: While diffusion models excel at generating high-quality images, their tendency to memorize training data poses significant privacy and copyright risks. In this work, we for the first time identify that memorization induces internal numerical instability, often manifesting as visually ``broken'' artifacts. Inspired by stability analysis in numerical methods, we introduce empirical stability regions based on latent update norms to quantitatively characterize stable behavior during generation. Leveraging this, we propose a principled, on-the-fly framework for step-wise detection and adaptive mitigation. Our approach suppresses memorization without altering prompts or guidance, thereby preserving semantic fidelity and image quality. Extensive experiments on Stable Diffusion 1.4 demonstrate that our method achieves an AUC $>0.999$ detection performance and a $0.0\%$ memorization rate after mitigation with negligible overhead ($\approx0.01$s per image).

### [43] [EasyVFX: Frequency-Driven Decoupling for Resource-Efficient VFX Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22051)
*Yue Ma,Xu Ye,Qinghe Wang,Yucheng Wang,Hongyu Liu,Yinhan Zhang,Xinyu Wang,Yuanpeng Che,Shanhui Mo,Paul Liang,Fangneng Zhan,Qifeng Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EasyVFX 通过频域分解将视觉特效生成中的空间纹理与时间动态解耦，并结合 Freq-MoE 与测试时训练，在较少数据和算力下实现高保真 VFX 合成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高质量 VFX 生成通常依赖大规模数据和高昂计算资源，难点在于复杂空间纹理与时间动态的强耦合。论文希望降低学习难度、数据依赖和训练成本，使专业级 VFX 生成更易获得。

Method: 方法基于频域解耦：将高频成分视为空间外观细节，将低频成分视为全局运动动态。提出两阶段训练：第一阶段使用 Frequency-aware Mixture-of-Experts（Freq-MoE），通过软路由为不同频段分配专家以学习外观与运动先验；第二阶段引入带 Frequency-constraint Loss 的测试时训练，使模型能对未见特效进行约约 100 步的单 GPU 快速局部适配。

Result: 实验表明，EasyVFX 能生成结构一致、视觉质量较高的特效，并在严格资源约束下保持现实感和时序稳定性。

Conclusion: 频率感知学习与频域解耦可有效降低 VFX 生成的优化复杂度和资源门槛，是实现轻量化、高质量特效合成的有效方向。

Abstract: Generating high-fidelity visual effects (VFX) typically demands massive datasets and prohibitive computational power due to the intricate coupling of spatial textures and temporal dynamics. In this paper, we introduce EasyVFX, a resource-efficient framework that achieves realistic VFX synthesis under stringent constraints. Our core philosophy lies in frequency-domain decomposition: we observe that the complexity of VFX can be significantly mitigated by decoupling high-frequency components, which represent intricate spatial appearances, from low-frequency components that encapsulate global motion dynamics. This spectral disentanglement transforms a high-dimensional learning problem into manageable sub-tasks, thereby lowering the optimization barrier and reducing data dependency. Building upon this insight, we propose a two-stage training paradigm. First, we design a Frequency-aware Mixture-of-Experts (Freq-MoE) architecture. By utilizing a soft routing mechanism, our model assigns specialized experts to distinct spectral bands, enabling them to cultivate robust priors for appearance and motion dynamics. This specialization allows the model to acquire foundational VFX knowledge with fewer GPU resources. Second, we introduce a Test-Time Training strategy powered by a novel Frequency-constraint Loss. This allows the pre-trained model to swiftly adapt to specific, unseen effects through localized optimizations, requiring only about 100 steps on a single GPU. Experimental results demonstrate that EasyVFX produces structurally consistent and visually stunning effects, proving that frequency-aware learning is a key catalyst for democratizing professional-grade VFX.
