### [202] [Towards Direct Evaluation of Harness Optimizers via Priority Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22505)
*Kai Tzu-iunn Ong,Minseok Kang,Dongwook Choi,Junhee Cho,Seungju Kim,Seungwon Lim,Geunha Jang,Minwoo Oh,Bogyung Jeong,Sunghwan Kim,Taeyoon Kwon,Jinyoung Yeo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出用“优先级排序”直接评估 harness optimizer 的逐步优化能力，并构建 Shor 基准验证其与真实多步优化效果相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 harness optimization 研究主要通过目标 agent 最终性能提升来间接评价 optimizer，忽略中间更新动作是否合理；这些动作可能错误并损害性能，因此难以判断优化来自有信息的决策还是试错。同时，由于缺少 oracle harness，直接评估 optimizer 成本高且不易实施。

Method: 作者设计了低成本的直接评估任务：让 harness optimizer 对给定 harness 中的组件（如工具）按“更新后可能提升或阻碍 agent 性能的潜力”进行排序，从而在步骤级量化其判断能力，无需昂贵 rollout 或人工逐项检查。该评估由 Shor 支撑，Shor 包含 182 个经人工验证的优化场景，覆盖不同领域、设计和时间阶段。

Result: 实验表明，optimizer 在优先级排序任务中的表现与其在真实多步 harness optimization 中提升 agent 的能力相关，因此该任务可作为优化能力的可靠预测指标。

Conclusion: 优先级排序为 harness optimizer 提供了一种简单、低成本且直接的评估方式，弥补了仅看最终性能提升的不足；Shor 基准进一步推动了对 optimizer 中间决策质量的系统评估。

Abstract: Harness optimization enables automated agent creation by having an optimizer agent iteratively update the harness of target agents. Despite its success, current studies evaluate optimizers solely by observing target agents' performance gains. This indirect end-improvement evaluation neglects optimizers' actions at intermediate steps, which are often erroneous and hinder agent performance. Therefore, it is unclear whether harness optimization is driven by optimizers' informed update actions or simply trial-and-error. This necessitates direct evaluation of harness optimizers. However, evaluating harness optimizers directly is non-trivial and costly due to the lack of oracle harnesses. To address this, we present a simple, low-cost design to directly evaluate them, namely priority ranking. By asking harness optimizers to rank components (e.g., tools) in a given harness by their potential to improve/hinder agent performance when updated, our design quantifies optimizer ability at the step level without expensive rollouts or manual examination. More importantly, optimizers' ranking performance correlates with their ability to improve agents in actual multi-step harness optimization, establishing priority ranking as a reliable predictor of optimization ability. Priority ranking is enabled by Shor, a collection of 182 human-verified optimization scenarios spanning across domains, designs, and time stages. Codes and data can be found at https://github.com/k59118/Harness_Optimizer_Evaluation.

</details>


### [203] [Search-E1: Self-Distillation Drives Self-Evolution in Search-Augmented Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22511)
*Zihan Liang,Yufei Ma,Ben Chen,Zhipeng Qian,Xuxin Zhang,Huangyu Dai,Lingtao Mao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Search-E1：一种不依赖外部强模型监督、辅助奖励模型/评论器、树搜索或手工奖励塑形的搜索增强推理智能体自进化方法，仅用标准 GRPO 与离线自蒸馏交替训练，在多个问答基准上取得较强表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有搜索增强推理智能体的后训练方法通常通过引入外部监督、过程奖励模型、回溯评论器、树搜索、多阶段课程或手工奖励设计来提升性能，但这些组件会显著增加训练复杂度，并依赖特定资源与工程设计。作者希望验证这些额外机制是否必要。

Method: 提出 Search-E1。方法在每轮 vanilla GRPO 训练后，让当前策略在训练问题上自行生成 rollout；随后使用离线自蒸馏（OFSD），通过 token-level forward KL 目标，将模型在普通推理上下文中的分布对齐到其在特权上下文下的分布。该特权上下文暴露一个更高效的 sibling trajectory，从而在无需外部监督的情况下提供较密集的逐步监督信号。

Result: 在七个问答基准上，使用 Qwen2.5-3B 时 Search-E1 达到 0.440 平均 EM，超过两个模型规模下所有开源基线。

Conclusion: 结果表明，搜索增强推理智能体的性能提升不一定依赖复杂外部模块或手工设计奖励；通过简单的 GRPO 与离线自蒸馏交替机制，模型可以实现有效的自我改进，并获得具有竞争力的问答表现。

Abstract: Post-training has become the dominant recipe for turning a language model into a competent search-augmented reasoning agent. A line of recent work pushes its performance further by adding elaborate machinery on top of this standard pipeline. These augmentations import external supervision from stronger external systems, attach auxiliary modules such as process reward models or retrospective critics, restructure the rollout itself with tree search or multi-stage curricula, or shape the reward with hand-crafted bonuses and penalties. Each addition delivers a measurable gain, but each also inflates the training pipeline and ties the recipe to resources or designs that may not always be available. We take a step back and ask whether any of this machinery is actually necessary, and propose Search-E1, a self-evolution method that lets a search-augmented agent improve through only vanilla GRPO interleaved with offline self-distillation (OFSD). After each GRPO round, the policy rolls out on its own training questions. A token-level forward KL objective then aligns the policy's inference-time distribution to its own distribution under a privileged context that exposes a more efficient sibling trajectory. Despite this simplicity, the procedure naturally provides dense per-step supervision. On seven QA benchmarks, Search-E1 reaches $0.440$ average EM with Qwen2.5-3B, surpassing all open-source baselines at both scales. Code and complete version will be made public soon.

</details>

TL;DR: 论文提出一种动态定量保障方法，将静态安全论证与运行时证据结合，用主观逻辑持续更新安全置信度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于主观逻辑构建统一的保障案例，将开发生命周期中的设计时证据与窗口化运行时安全性能指标（SPI）结合；运行时持续评估SPI证据，并针对相关声明更新置信度：无违规时逐步提升置信度，发生违规时快速施加惩罚。该更新规则强调安全响应性，而非严格遵循经典贝叶斯后验更新。

Result: 作者通过一个仿真的施工区域辅助功能进行演示，重点考察基于机器学习的施工锥检测组件，展示了系统在运行过程中随着SPI证据被观察到，相关安全置信度如何动态演化。

Conclusion: 该方法表明，将设计时证据与运行时SPI纳入同一主观逻辑安全案例，可以实现面向运行状态的动态量化保障，尤其适合需要持续监测机器学习组件安全表现的系统。

Abstract: We present a method for dynamic quantitative assurance that enhances static safety cases with continuous, runtime-driven confidence updates. The method quantifies and propagates confidence across the development lifecycle by integrating design-time evidence and windowed runtime Safety Performance Indicators (SPIs) within a single Subjective Logic (SL)-based assurance case. At runtime, SPI evidence is continuously evaluated, and targeted claims are updated using a rule that increases confidence in the absence of violations and imposes prompt penalties when violations occur. This design prioritizes safety-relevant responsiveness over exact classical Bayesian posterior updates. We demonstrate the method using a simulation-based construction zone assist function, focusing on an ML-based construction cone detection component, and show how confidence evolves as SPI evidence is observed in operation.

### [205] [TerminalWorld: Benchmarking Agents on Real-World Terminal Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22535)
*Zhaoyang Chu,Jiarui Hu,Xingyu Jiang,Pengyu Zou,Han Li,Chao Peng,Peter O'Hearn,Earl T. Barr,Mark Harman,Federica Sarro,He Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TerminalWorld 是一个从真实终端录屏自动反向构造高保真评测任务的数据引擎，并形成包含 1,530 个任务的终端智能体基准；实验显示当前前沿模型/智能体在真实终端工作流上仍表现有限，最高通过率仅 62.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有终端智能体评测多依赖专家人工设计任务，可能覆盖面有限、真实性不足，且难以随开发者实践变化而扩展。论文希望构建一种可规模化、贴近真实使用场景的终端任务评测体系。

Method: 作者提出 TerminalWorld 引擎，从 80,870 条真实终端录屏中自动反向工程生成评测任务，经过验证得到 1,530 个任务，覆盖 18 类真实场景、1,280 个独特命令，并人工审查抽取 200 个代表性任务组成 TerminalWorld-Verified 子集。随后在该子集上评测 8 个前沿模型和 6 个智能体。

Result: TerminalWorld-Verified 上当前系统表现仍不理想，最高通过率为 62.5%。该基准与现有专家构建基准 Terminal-Bench 的分数相关性较弱，Pearson r=0.20，说明其捕捉到不同的真实终端能力维度。

Conclusion: TerminalWorld 通过自动化、真实数据驱动的方式提供了更具真实性和可扩展性的终端智能体评测框架，可用于持续评估智能体在不断变化的真实开发终端环境中的能力。

Abstract: We introduce TerminalWorld, a scalable data engine that automatically reverse-engineers high-fidelity evaluation tasks from "in-the-wild" terminal recordings. Processing 80,870 terminal recordings, the engine yields a full benchmark of 1,530 validated tasks, spanning 18 real-world categories, ranging from short everyday operations to workflows exceeding 50 steps, and covering 1,280 unique commands. From these, we curate a Verified subset of 200 representative, manually reviewed tasks. Comprehensive benchmarking on TerminalWorld-Verified across eight frontier models and six agents reveals that current systems still struggle with authentic terminal workflows, achieving a maximum pass rate of only 62.5%. Moreover, TerminalWorld captures real-world terminal capabilities distinct from existing expert-curated benchmarks (e.g., Terminal-Bench), with only a weak correlation to their scores (Pearson r=0.20). The automated engine makes TerminalWorld authentic and scalable by construction, enabling it to evaluate agents in real-world terminal environments as developer practices evolve. Data and code are available at https://github.com/EuniAI/TerminalWorld.

### [206] [Think Thrice Before You Speak: Dual knowledge-enhanced Theory-of-Mind Reasoning for Persuasive Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22602)
*Minghui Ma,Bin Guo,Runze Yang,Mengqi Chen,Yan Liu,Jingqi Liu,Yahan Pei,Xuehao Ma,Qiuyun Zhang,Zhiwen Yu*

Abstract: Persuasive dialogue requires reasoning about others' latent mental states, a capability known as Theory of Mind (ToM). However, due to reliance on simple prompting strategies and insufficient ToM knowledge, existing LLMs often fail to capture the intrinsic dependencies among mental states, leading to fragmented representations and unstable reasoning. To address these challenges, we introduce the ToM-based Persuasive Dialogue (ToM-PD) task, grounded in the Belief-Desire-Intention (BDI) framework, which explicitly models the sequential dependencies among mental states in multi-turn dialogues. To facilitate research on this task, we construct a large-scale annotated dataset, ToM-based Broad Persuasive Dialogues (ToM-BPD), capturing fine-grained mental states and corresponding persuasive strategies. We further propose Think Thrice Before You Speak (TTBYS), a knowledge-enhanced stepwise reasoning framework that leverages both explicit and implicit prior experiences to improve LLMs' inference of desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that Qwen3-8B equipped with TTBYS outperforms GPT-5 by 1.20%, 22.80%, and 16.97% in predicting desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies, respectively. Case studies further show that our approach enhances interpretability and consistency in reasoning.

Most existing spreadsheet agents rely on specialized prompting over general-purpose LLMs; while this design has potentials on simple spreadsheet operations, it struggles to manage the complex, multi-step workflows typical of real-world applications.
  We introduce Spreadsheet-RL, a reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning framework designed to train specialized spreadsheet agents within a realistic Microsoft Excel environment. Spreadsheet-RL features an automated pipeline for scalable collection of paired start-goal spreadsheets from online forums, as well as domain-specific evaluation tasks in areas such as finance and supply chain management, which we compile into the new Domain-Spreadsheet benchmark dataset. Through comprehensive experiments, we show that Spreadsheet-RL substantially enhances AI agent's performance on both general and domain-specific spreadsheet tasks: it improves Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507's Pass@1 on SpreadsheetBench from 12.0% to 23.4%, and raises Pass@1 from 8.4% to 17.2% on our curated Domain-Spreadsheet dataset. *Hanjun Luo,Zhimu Huang,Sylvia Chung,Yiran Wang,Yingbin Jin,Jialin Li,Jiang Li,Xinfeng Li,Hanan Salam*

TL;DR: 本文提出 AtelierEval，用于评估人类或多模态大语言模型作为上游提示词生成者的提示能力，并提出 AtelierJudge 作为自动化评估器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本生成图像评测通常固定提示词，只评估 T2I 模型本身，忽略了上游提示者将用户意图转化为高质量详细提示词的能力，因此缺少统一、可量化的提示能力基准。

Method: 作者构建包含 360 个专家设计任务的 AtelierEval，覆盖三类任务，并基于真实世界挑战分类法设计任务，同时支持人类和 MLLM 接口；此外提出技能导向、带记忆增强的智能体评估器 AtelierJudge，对提示词-图像对给出主观与客观评分。

Result: AtelierJudge 与人类专家评分的 Spearman 相关系数达到 0.79，接近人类评估水平；实验比较了 8 个 MLLM、48 名人类用户和 4 个 T2I 后端，验证了 AtelierEval 的诊断有效性，并发现模仿策略优于规划策略。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了上游提示能力评估的空白，提供了可扩展、可靠的统一基准与自动评估器，并指出未来提示器发展应更多利用图像增强方向。

Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) systems increasingly rely on upstream prompters, either humans or multimodal large language models (MLLMs), to translate user intent into detailed prompts. Yet current benchmarks fix the prompt and only evaluate T2I models, leaving the prompting proficiency of this upstream component entirely unmeasured. We introduce AtelierEval, the first unified benchmark that quantifies prompting proficiency across 360 expert-crafted tasks. Grounded in a cognitive view, it spans three task categories and instantiates tasks using a taxonomy of real-world challenges, with a dual interface for both humans and MLLMs. To enable scalable and reliable evaluation, we propose AtelierJudge, a skill-based, memory-augmented agentic evaluator. It produces subjective and objective scores for prompt-image pairs, achieving a Spearman correlation of 0.79 with human experts, approaching human performance. Extensive experiments benchmark 8 MLLMs against 48 human users across 4 T2I backends, validate AtelierEval as a robust diagnostic tool, and reveal the superiority of mimicry over planning, advocating for an image-augmented direction for future prompters. Our work is released to support future research.

</details>


### [209] [Claw AI Lab: An Autonomous Multi-Agent Research Team](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22662)
*Fan Wu,Cheng Chen,Zhenshan Tan,Taiyu Zhang,Xinzhen Xu,Yanyu Qian,Dingcheng Gao,Lanyun Zhu,Qi Zhu,Yi Tan,Deyi Ji,Guosheng Lin,Tianrun Chen,Deheng Ye,Fayao Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文提出 Claw AI Lab：用户可通过一个提示实例化包含自定义角色的研究团队，支持协作工作流、实时监控、产物检查、回滚与恢复；同时提供探索、多智能体讨论和复现等研究模式。核心组件 Claw-Code Harness 将本地代码库、数据集和检查点连接到可运行实验，并将执行产物反馈至研究循环。

Result: 在五个 AI 研究案例的内部评估中，相比 AutoResearchClaw 基线，AI 专家评审更偏好 Claw AI Lab，认为其在想法新颖性、实验完整性和论文呈现质量方面表现更好。

Conclusion: Claw AI Lab 展示了自动化科研平台向可用、交互式、可靠性意识强的科学基础设施演进的早期方向，尤其强调过程可控性、实验完整性和结果可信转化。

Abstract: We present Claw AI Lab, a lab-native autonomous research platform that advances automated research from a hidden prompt-to-paper pipeline into an interactive AI laboratory. Rather than centering the system around a single agent or a fixed serial workflow, we allow users to instantiate a full research team from one prompt, with customizable roles, collaborative workflows, real-time monitoring, artifact inspection, and rollback/resume control through a unified dashboard. The platform also supports distinct research modes for exploration, multi-agent discussion, and reproduction, making autonomous research substantially more steerable and laboratory-like in practice. A key practical contribution of Claw AI Lab lies in its Claw-Code Harness, which connects local codebases, datasets, and checkpoints to runnable experiments and feeds execution artifacts back into the research loop. As a result, the harness improves not only execution integration, but also experimental completion and result integrity: experiments are easier to inspect, iterate on, and faithfully transfer into final papers, reducing common failure modes such as partial runs and malformed result reporting. In our internal evaluation on five AI research case studies, using AutoResearchClaw as the baseline, Claw AI Lab is consistently preferred by AI expert judges on idea novelty, experiment completeness, and paper presentation quality. We view Claw AI Lab as an early step toward a new paradigm: autonomous research as usable, interactive, and reliability-aware scientific infrastructure.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有电子表格基准多关注问答或单公式编辑，无法衡量智能体从高层指令出发构建完整电子表格的能力；而企业金融场景需要可审阅、可修改、格式专业且计算准确的完整交付物。

Result: Claude系列在基准中表现领先，并在定性审查中生成最具专业外观的电子表格；但即使最强模型也经常低于专业金融标准，且任务难度超过少数链式计算后性能显著下降。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly expected to carry out end-to-end workflows, producing complete artifacts from high-level user instructions. To meet enterprise needs, frontier AI labs have developed agents that can construct entire spreadsheets from scratch. This is especially relevant in finance, where core workflows such as financial modeling, forecasting, and scenario analysis are commonly conducted through spreadsheets. Yet, existing spreadsheet benchmarks do not measure this advanced capability, focusing instead on question-answering or single-formula edits. To address this gap, we provide one of the first evaluations of agents on end-to-end spreadsheet tasks, focusing on economically critical financial workflows such as modeling and scenario analysis. Since deliverables therein are routinely reviewed and revised by multiple stakeholders, judging their quality necessarily involves high-level criteria such as readability or ease of modification. To reflect the multidimensional nature of solution quality, we develop an evaluation taxonomy comprising three dimensions: Accuracy, Formula, and Format, each comprising fine-grained criteria that reflect professional standards. The Claude family leads the benchmark and produces the most professional-looking outputs in our qualitative review, but even the strongest agents frequently fall short of professional finance standards and degrade sharply as the difficulty increases beyond a few chained calculations. This suggests that current agents are not yet able to reliably produce professional-quality spreadsheets at the level of complexity real-world workflows demand.

### [211] [Is Capability a Liability? More Capable Language Models Make Worse Forecasts When It Matters Most](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22672)
*Nick Merrill,Jaeho Lee,Ezra Karger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现，在具有超线性增长和尾部制度转换风险的时间序列预测任务中，更强的大语言模型反而给出更差的分布式预测；该问题主要集中在上尾部，并会被常见单阈值指标掩盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融、流行病等领域的预测对象常呈现超线性增长与尾部风险。现有LLM预测评测常依赖二元阈值指标，可能无法揭示模型在尾部风险和分布校准上的真实缺陷，因此需要系统检验模型能力提升是否一定带来更好预测。

Method: 作者构建并发布无污染的模拟世界基准ForecastBench-Sim，在合成SIR流行病预测及匹配线性对照上测试LLM；同时在COVID-19、麻疹、房地产市场和恶性通胀等真实数据集上复现结果。通过分位数层面的误差分解分析失败来源，并在Llama-3.1家族内考察模型规模与后训练的独立影响；比较单阈值指标与包含尾部的连续无界评分。

Result: 更强模型在这些任务上产生更差的分布预测，逆向缩放现象主要发生在上尾部：更强模型倾向将高分位预测上移以追随激进增长外推，而低尾部基本不变。模型规模和后训练均会独立加剧该效应；领域知识不能稳定恢复校准。常见单阈值指标不会显示该逆向缩放，甚至会在相同输出上反转能力—准确性关系的符号。

Conclusion: LLM在高增长和尾部风险时间序列预测中可能随能力增强而校准变差，尤其在上尾部风险估计上。评测不应只依赖有界二元阈值指标，而应同时采用连续、无界且覆盖尾部误差的准确性度量，以避免低估高风险预测失败。

Abstract: We document inverse scaling in LLMs on forecasting problems whose underlying time series exhibit superlinear growth and tail risk of regime change, a structure common in finance and epidemiology. On these tasks, more capable models produce worse distributional forecasts. The pattern appears on ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim), a contamination-free, simulated-world benchmark we release, in forecasting synthetic SIR epidemics with a matched linear control, and replicates in real-world datasets on COVID-19, measles, housing markets, and hyperinflation. A per-quantile decomposition shows the failure concentrates at the upper tail, which more capable models shift upward to track aggressive extrapolations of growth, while the lower tail stays put. A within-family study of Llama-3.1 shows that both model scale and post-training independently contribute to this effect. Domain knowledge does not reliably rescue calibration. This inverse scaling does not appear on single-threshold metrics common in LLM forecasting benchmarks, reversing the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on identical outputs. Single-threshold scoring at conventional cutoffs misses the upper-tail cost; tail-inclusive scoring reverses the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on the same outputs. We recommend that LLM forecasting evaluations use continuous (and unbounded) measures of accuracy alongside bounded binary threshold metrics.

### [212] [Forecasting Scientific Progress with Artificial Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22681)
*Sean Wu,Pan Lu,Yupeng Chen,Jonathan Bragg,Yutaro Yamada,Peter Clark,David Clifton,Philip Torr,James Zou,Junchi Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 CUSP 基准，用时间截断和受控知识条件评估 AI 预测科学进展的能力；结果显示当前前沿模型能识别合理方向，但难以可靠判断突破是否会发生及何时发生，并存在过度自信和偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI 正越来越多参与科学发现，但其是否具备“预见”科学进展的能力尚不明确。作者希望在严格控制模型可访问知识、尤其是时间信息的条件下，评估 AI 对未来科学事件的预测能力，而不是仅测试其对已知知识的记忆。

Method: 作者构建 CUSP（Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress），一个跨学科、事件级科学预测基准，包含 4,760 个科学事件。评估维度包括可行性判断、机制推理、生成式方案设计和时间预测，并通过训练截止时间、预截止知识、完整信息等条件比较模型表现。

Result: 当前前沿模型表现出系统性且因领域而异的局限：能从候选方向中识别较合理的研究方向，但不能可靠预测科学进展是否会实现，也常系统性误判发生时间。AI 领域进展的时间相对更可预测，而生物、化学、物理更难。事件是否位于训练截止时间前后对表现影响不大；额外预截止知识有帮助但不能达到完整信息条件，尤其对高引用成果差距更明显。模型还存在过度自信和强响应偏置。

Conclusion: 当前 AI 系统尚不能作为可靠的科学进展预测工具。已有知识访问并不自动转化为前瞻性预测能力，模型更多受益于事件发生后的信息，而非真正的前向推断；其不确定性估计也不可靠。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is increasingly embedded in scientific discovery, yet whether it can anticipate scientific progress remains unclear. To study this question, we introduce a temporally grounded evaluation framework for forecasting scientific progress under controlled knowledge constraints. We present CUSP (Cutoff-conditioned Unseen Scientific Progress), a multi-disciplinary and event-level benchmark that evaluates scientific forecasting in AI systems through feasibility assessment, mechanistic reasoning, generative solution design, and temporal prediction. Across 4,760 scientific events, we observe systematic and domain-dependent limitations in current frontier models. While models can identify plausible research directions from competing candidates, they fail to reliably predict whether scientific advances will be realized and systematically misestimate when they will occur. Performance is highly heterogeneous across domains, with the timing of AI progress more predictable than advances in biology, chemistry, and physics. Performance is largely insensitive to whether events occur before or after the training cutoff, suggesting these limitations cannot be explained solely by knowledge exposure in training data. Under controlled information access, additional pre-cutoff knowledge improves performance but does not close the gap to full-information settings, which becomes more pronounced for high-citation advances. Models also exhibit systematic overconfidence and strong response biases, indicating unreliable uncertainty estimation. Taken together, current AI systems fall short as predictive tools for scientific progress. Access to prior knowledge does not translate into reliable forecasting, and performance benefits more from post-event information than from forward-looking prediction.

### [213] [AMEL: Accumulated Message Effects on LLM Judgments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22714)
*Sid-ali Temkit*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究对话历史中先前评价的正负极性是否会系统性偏移大语言模型后续判断，发现模型会向历史主导极性偏移，负面历史影响更强；建议评测流水线尽量每个样本使用新上下文。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型常被用作自动评估器，在同一对话中连续审查代码、审核内容或给输出打分。若先前对话的评价倾向会影响后续判断，将威胁批量评测的公平性与可靠性，因此作者提出并检验“累积消息效应”（AMEL）。

Method: 作者在75,898次API调用中测试来自4个提供方的11个模型，将相同测试项分别置于孤立上下文，或置于以正面/负面评价为主的历史对话之后，比较判断偏移。进一步分析不确定性水平、上下文长度、负面不对称、模型规模，以及token概率分布、语义因素和偏置消息位置的影响。

Result: 模型判断会向既有对话极性偏移，整体效应显著（d=-0.17, p<10^-46）。高不确定样本效应更强（d=-0.34），确定性样本较弱（d=-0.15）。偏差不随上下文长度增长，5轮与50轮历史效果相近。负面历史诱导的偏差约为正面历史的1.62倍。更大模型偏差较小但仍存在。后续实验显示偏移是连续的token概率变化，位置不重要，负面不对称包含token层与语义层因素。

Conclusion: LLM作为评估器时存在由历史评价极性引发的系统性上下文偏差，尤其影响本来不确定的判断，并且负面历史更具影响力。最直接的工程缓解方式是每个评测项使用独立新上下文；若必须批处理，应尽量平衡历史中的正负倾向。

Abstract: Large language models are routinely used as automated evaluators: to review code, moderate content, or score outputs, often with many items passing through one conversation. We ask whether the polarity of prior conversation history biases subsequent judgments, an effect we call the accumulated message effect on LLM judgments (AMEL). Across 75,898 API calls to 11 models from 4 providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, and four open-source models), we present identical test items in isolation or following histories saturated with predominantly positive or negative evaluations.
  Models shift toward the conversation's prevailing polarity (d = -0.17, p < 10^-46). The effect concentrates on items where the model is genuinely uncertain at baseline (d = -0.34 for high-entropy items, vs d = -0.15 when the baseline is deterministic). Bias does not grow with context length: 5 prior turns and 50 produce the same shift (Spearman |r| < 0.01; OLS slope p = 0.80). And there is a negativity asymmetry: paired per item, negative histories induce 1.62x more bias than positive (t = 13.46, p < 10^-39, n = 2,481). Scaling helps but does not solve it (Anthropic: Haiku -0.22 to Opus -0.17; OpenAI: Nano -0.34 to GPT-5.2 -0.17).
  Three follow-ups narrow the mechanism. The token probability distribution shifts continuously, not at a threshold. The negativity asymmetry has both token-level and semantic components, though attributing the balance is exploratory at our sample sizes. Position does not matter: five biased turns anywhere in a 50-turn history produce the same shift. The simplest fix for evaluation pipelines is a fresh context per item; when batching is unavoidable, balancing the history helps.

</details>

*Jorge Fandinno,Yuliya Lierler,Torsten Schaub*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 ASP 在大型知识表示与推理任务中需要更好的结构化、复用和实例化机制；现有非模块语义难以充分刻画 clingo 中通过子程序与参数进行组织的实践特性。

Method: 作者引入“参数化模块逻辑程序”形式体系，允许定义带参数的子程序，并通过内涵性声明规定谓词的定义范围；随后用该体系刻画带有 collective control 的 clingo 程序语义，并建立其理论基础。

Result: 该形式化能够表达和解释 clingo 程序的模块化结构、子程序实例化及其语义，同时展示了模块化 ASP 与传统非模块 ASP 之间的联系。

Conclusion: 参数化模块逻辑程序为一阶 ASP 的模块化提供了清晰的理论框架，有助于提高程序结构化、可复用性和语义可解释性，并为实践系统与经典 ASP 语义之间搭建桥梁。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore the concept of modularity in first-order answer set programming (ASP). We provide theoretical foundations for modular ASP, illustrate its usefulness, and connect to traditional non-modular ASP.

Abstract: AI models are already deployed in societies affected by armed conflict, and journalists, humanitarian workers, governments and ordinary citizens rely on them for information or for their work processes. No established practice exists for checking whether their outputs can make those conflicts worse. We tested nine model configurations from four providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, DeepSeek, xAI) on 90 multi-turn scenarios designed to surface misaligned behaviour in conflict contexts: false equivalence between documented atrocities, denial of genocide, and failure to recognise ethnic slurs, among others. When such outputs feed into journalism, humanitarian reporting, or public debate, they can deepen divisions in fragile societies. Failure rates span 6\% to 47\% between the best and worst performing models, which makes model choice a safety question in its own right and when users pushed for ``balance'' in cases where international courts have already assigned responsibility, five of nine configurations failed 80 to 100 percent of the time. We release the first evaluation framework for this domain and propose adding it to alignment evaluation portfolios.

### [216] [Beyond Acoustic Emotion Recognition: Multimodal Pathos Analysis in Political Speech Using LLM-Based and Acoustic Emotion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22732)
*Juergen Dietrich*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Method: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Result: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Abstract: We investigate whether acoustic emotion recognition models can serve as proxies for the Pathos dimension in political speech analysis, as operationalised by the TRUST multi-agent large language model (LLM) pipeline. Using a Bundestag plenary speech by Felix Banaszak (51 segments, 245 s) as a case study, we compare three analysis modalities: (1) emotion2vec_plus_large, an acoustic speech emotion recognition (SER) model whose continuous Arousal and Valence values are derived via post-hoc Russell Circumplex projection; (2) Gemini 2.5 Flash, an LLM analysing the full speech audio together with its transcript in an open-ended, context-aware fashion; and (3) TRUST-Pathos scores from a three-advocate LLM supervisor ensemble. Spearman rank correlations reveal that Gemini Valence correlates strongly with TRUST-Pathos (rho = +0.664, p < 0.001), whereas emotion2vec Valence does not (rho = +0.097, p = 0.499). We further demonstrate, via a systematic quality evaluation of the Berlin Database of Emotional Speech (EMO-DB) using Gemini in an open-ended annotation paradigm, that standard SER benchmark corpora suffer from acted speech, cultural bias, and category incompatibility. Our results suggest that LLM-based multimodal analysis captures semantically defined political emotion substantially better than acoustic models alone, while acoustic features remain informative for low-level Arousal estimation. Future work will extend this approach to video-based analysis incorporating facial expression and gaze.

### [217] [Advancing Mathematics Research with AI-Driven Formal Proof Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22763)
*George Tsoukalas,Anton Kovsharov,Sergey Shirobokov,Anja Surina,Moritz Firsching,Gergely Bérczi,Francisco J. R. Ruiz,Arun Suggala,Adam Zsolt Wagner,Eric Wieser,Lei Yu,Aja Huang,Miklós Z. Horváth,Andrew Ferrauiolo,Henryk Michalewski,Codrut Grosu,Thomas Hubert,Matej Balog,Pushmeet Kohli,Swarat Chaudhuri*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文大规模评估了利用大语言模型生成 Lean 形式化证明来解决开放数学问题的能力，结果显示最强智能体可自主解决部分开放问题与猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在数学推理上表现提升，但可靠性不足限制其在数学研究中的应用；形式化证明可作为验证机制，缓解错误推理问题。

Method: 构建并评估 AI 辅助形式化证明搜索智能体，让其生成 Lean 证明并通过 Lean 验证；在开放 Erdős 问题和 OEIS 猜想等任务上进行大规模测试，并比较高级智能体与基础“生成—验证”交替策略的成本与效果。

Result: 最强智能体以每题数百美元量级成本自主解决了 353 个开放 Erdős 问题中的 9 个，并证明了 492 个 OEIS 猜想中的 44 个；基础智能体也复现了 Erdős 问题成果，但在最难问题上成本更高。

Conclusion: AI 辅助的形式化证明搜索已具备解决部分开放数学问题的能力；智能体设计显著影响效率与成本，该方向对组合数学、优化、图论、代数几何和量子光学等研究具有应用潜力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly excel at mathematical reasoning, but their unreliability limits their utility in mathematics research. A mitigation is using LLMs to generate formal proofs in languages like Lean. We perform the first large-scale evaluation of this method's ability to solve open problems. Our most capable agent autonomously resolved 9 of 353 open Erdős problems at the per-problem cost of a few hundred dollars, proved 44/492 OEIS conjectures, and is being deployed in combinatorics, optimization, graph theory, algebraic geometry, and quantum optics research. A basic agent alternating LLM-based generation with Lean-based verification replicated the Erdős successes but proved costlier on the hardest problems. These findings demonstrate the power of AI-aided formal proof search and shed light on the agent designs that enable it.

</details>


### [218] [LCGuard: Latent Communication Guard for Safe KV Sharing in Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22786)
*Sadia Asif,Mohammad Mohammadi Amiri,Momin Abbas,Prasanna Sattigeri,Karthikeyan Natesan Ramamurthy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 LCGuard，用于在多智能体大语言模型中保障基于 KV cache 的潜在通信安全，通过表示级变换降低敏感信息可重构性，同时尽量保留任务语义与性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体 LLM 系统越来越依赖中间通信协作。相比自然语言通信，基于 Transformer KV cache 的潜在通信可提升效率并保留更丰富的任务信息，但 KV cache 也可能携带上下文输入、中间推理状态和智能体特有信息，形成不透明的敏感信息泄漏通道。

Method: 作者将共享 KV cache 视为潜在工作记忆，在跨智能体传输前学习表示级变换。论文以“能否被对抗解码器重构出敏感输入”作为敏感信息泄漏的操作化定义，并构建对抗训练框架：解码器尝试重构敏感输入，LCGuard 则学习在保留任务相关语义的同时降低可重构信息。

Result: 在多个模型系列和多智能体基准上的实验表明，LCGuard 相比标准 KV-sharing 基线能持续降低基于重构的泄漏和攻击成功率，同时保持有竞争力的任务表现。

Conclusion: LCGuard 为 KV cache 潜在通信提供了一种表示级安全机制，说明通过对抗式表示变换可以在多智能体协作效率、语义保真和隐私防护之间取得较好平衡。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent systems increasingly rely on intermediate communication to coordinate complex tasks. While most existing systems communicate through natural language, recent work shows that latent communication, particularly through transformer key-value (KV) caches, can improve efficiency and preserve richer task-relevant information. However, KV caches also encode contextual inputs, intermediate reasoning states, and agent-specific information, creating an opaque channel through which sensitive content may propagate across agents without explicit textual disclosure. To address this, we introduce \textbf{LCGuard} (Latent Communication Guard), a framework for safe KV-based latent communication in multi-agent LLM systems. LCGuard treats shared KV caches as latent working memory and learns representation-level transformations before cache artifacts are transmitted across agents. We formalize representation-level sensitive information leakage operationally through reconstruction: a shared cache artifact is unsafe if an adversarial decoder can recover agent-specific sensitive inputs from it. This leads to an adversarial training formulation in which the adversary learns to reconstruct sensitive inputs, while LCGuard learns transformations that preserve task-relevant semantics and reduce reconstructable information. Empirical evaluations across multiple model families and multi-agent benchmarks show that LCGuard consistently reduces reconstruction-based leakage and attack success rates while maintaining competitive task performance compared to standard KV-sharing baselines.

</details>


### [219] [Gated DeltaNet-2: Decoupling Erase and Write in Linear Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22791)
*Ali Hatamizadeh,Yejin Choi,Jan Kautz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Gated DeltaNet-2，一种线性注意力/Delta-rule 模型，通过将“擦除旧内容”和“写入新内容”的门控解耦为逐通道 erase gate 与 write gate，在保持高效训练与推理的同时提升长上下文检索和语言建模表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性注意力用固定大小递归状态替代 softmax attention 的无界缓存，可实现线性时间序列混合和常数内存解码；但压缩记忆的关键难题是如何在不破坏既有关联的情况下编辑记忆。已有 Delta-rule、Gated DeltaNet 与 KDA 虽引入读出抵消、自适应遗忘和逐通道衰减，但仍用单一标量门同时控制 key 侧擦除与 value 侧写入，限制了记忆编辑的灵活性。

Method: 提出 Gated Delta Rule-2：使用逐通道擦除门 b_t 控制旧内容在 key 侧的移除，使用逐通道写入门 w_t 控制新 value 内容的提交；继承自适应遗忘与逐通道衰减。作者给出 fast-weight update 视角，设计将逐通道衰减吸收到非对称 erase factors 中的 chunkwise WY 算法，并推导 gate-aware backward pass，以支持高效并行训练。

Result: 在 1.3B 参数、100B FineWeb-Edu tokens 训练设置下，Gated DeltaNet-2 在语言建模、常识推理和检索任务上相较 Mamba-2、Gated DeltaNet、KDA、Mamba-3 变体取得最强综合结果；在长上下文 RULER needle-in-a-haystack 多键检索基准上优势最明显，并在 recurrent 与 hybrid 设置中均保持较强表现。

Conclusion: Gated DeltaNet-2 通过解耦擦除与写入门控，解决了既有 DeltaNet/KDA 中标量门绑定的问题，在不牺牲线性注意力效率的前提下增强了压缩记忆编辑能力，尤其适合长上下文和多键检索场景。

Abstract: Linear attention replaces the unbounded cache of softmax attention with a fixed-size recurrent state, reducing sequence mixing to linear time and decoding to constant memory. The hard part is not just what to forget, but how to edit this compressed memory without scrambling existing associations. Delta-rule models subtract the current read before writing a new value, and Kimi Delta Attention (KDA) sharpens forgetting with channel-wise decay. But the active edit still uses a single scalar gate to control two different things: how much old content to erase on the key side and how much new content to commit on the value side. We introduce Gated DeltaNet-2, which generalizes both Gated DeltaNet and KDA by inheriting adaptive forgetting and channel-wise decay while addressing their shared limitation, the scalar tie between erasing and writing. Gated Delta Rule-2 separates these roles with a channel-wise erase gate b_t and a channel-wise write gate w_t, reducing to KDA when both gates collapse to the same scalar and to Gated DeltaNet when the decay also collapses. We derive a fast-weight update view, a chunkwise WY algorithm with channel-wise decay absorbed into asymmetric erase factors, and a gate-aware backward pass that preserves efficient parallel training. At 1.3B parameters trained on 100B FineWeb-Edu tokens, Gated DeltaNet-2 achieves the strongest overall results among Mamba-2, Gated DeltaNet, KDA, and Mamba-3 variants across language modeling, commonsense reasoning, and retrieval. Its advantage is most pronounced on long-context RULER needle-in-a-haystack benchmarks, where it improves the evaluated multi-key retrieval setting and remains strong in both recurrent and hybrid settings. Code is available at https://github.com/NVlabs/GatedDeltaNet-2.

</details>


### [220] [MOSS: Self-Evolution through Source-Level Rewriting in Autonomous Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22794)
*Qianshu Cai,Yonggang Zhang,Xianzhang Jia,Wei Xue,Jun Song,Xinmei Tian,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 MOSS：一种让自主智能体在部署后基于生产失败证据进行源代码级自我重写与验证的系统，以修复文本层无法触及的结构性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自进化智能体通常只修改技能文件、提示词、记忆模式或工作流图等文本工件，无法触及路由、钩子顺序、状态不变量和调度等代码层结构，因此许多部署后的重复失败需要人工更新才能修复。

Method: MOSS 将生产失败证据自动整理成批次，经过确定性的多阶段演化流程；代码修改交由可插拔的外部编码智能体 CLI 完成，而系统本身控制阶段顺序与判定。候选版本在临时试验 worker 中通过批量回放验证，并在用户同意后通过原地容器替换上线，同时配合健康探针触发回滚。

Result: 在 OpenClaw 上，MOSS 在单轮无人工干预演化中将四项任务平均评分从 0.25 提升到 0.61。

Conclusion: 源代码级适应比文本工件修改更通用、更确定，也更能解决智能体系统的结构性故障；MOSS 展示了生产环境中自重写智能体的可行性。

Abstract: Autonomous agentic systems are largely static after deployment: they do not learn from user interactions, and recurring failures persist until the next human-driven update ships a fix. Self-evolving agents have emerged in response, but all confine evolution to text-mutable artifacts -- skill files, prompt configurations, memory schemas, workflow graphs -- and leave the agent harness untouched. Since routing, hook ordering, state invariants, and dispatch live in code rather than in any text artifact, an entire class of structural failure is physically unreachable from the text layer. We argue that source-level adaptation is a fundamentally more general medium: it is Turing-complete, a strict superset of every text-mutable scope, takes effect deterministically rather than through base-model compliance, and does not erode under long-context drift. We present MOSS, a system that performs self-rewriting at the source level on production agentic substrates. Each evolution is anchored to an automatically curated batch of production-failure evidence and proceeds through a deterministic multi-stage pipeline; code modification is delegated to a pluggable external coding-agent CLI while MOSS retains stage ordering and verdicts. Candidates are verified by replaying the batch against the candidate image in ephemeral trial workers, then promoted via user-consent-gated, in-place container swap with health-probe-gated rollback. On OpenClaw, MOSS lifts a four-task mean grader score from 0.25 to 0.61 in a single cycle without human intervention.

</details>

### [221] [Reed-Muller Codes for Joint Random and Stuck-At Error Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21727)
*Ivana Djurdjevic,Robert Mateescu,Cyril Guyot*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出一种面向含固定缺陷与随机错误存储器的块编码方案，通过递归构造掩码集合来屏蔽固定错误，并可结合 Reed-Muller 码纠正随机错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算机存储器中可能同时存在 stuck-at 固定缺陷和随机错误；编码器可获得缺陷位置/状态信息而解码器不可知，因此需要低冗余、低复杂度且无需解码器缺陷信息的编码方法来提升存储可靠性。

Method: 作者递归构造一组掩码，使其能够在长度为 2^m 的二进制序列中满足任意 s 个 stuck-at 错误（s≤m）。证明这些掩码属于 Reed-Muller 码 RM(s−1,m)，并用固定的掩码位子集唯一表示每个掩码；进一步将该 stuck-at 编码作为 RM(r,m)（r≥s−1）的子码，以支持随机错误纠正。

Result: 构造出的掩码集合规模不超过 2^s m^{s−1}；给出了 stuck-at 冗余大小的上下界。编码过程无需搜索掩码，可由递归构造直接完成；解码只需一次尝试，几乎不增加复杂度和延迟。

Conclusion: 该工作给出了一种非线性的 stuck-at 编码构造，在编码端利用缺陷边信息有效处理固定缺陷，同时可嵌入 Reed-Muller 框架以兼顾随机错误纠正，适合对复杂度和时延敏感的存储可靠性场景。

Abstract: Block codes are considered for improving the reliability of messages stored in a computer memory with both stuck-at defects and random errors. It is assumed that the side information about the state of the defects is available to the encoder, but not to the decoder. A novel recursive construction of a set of masks is developed such that it can satisfy any $s$ stuck-at errors in a $2^m$ binary sequence, when $s \leq m$. We prove that the masks generated in this way are codewords in a Reed-Muller $RM(s-1, m)$ code. The constructed set contains no more than $2^s m^{s-1}$ masks. We provide the lower and the upper bound on the size of the stuck-at redundancy, a fixed subset of mask bits that uniquely represents each mask in the set. The stuck-at code constructed in this way is a non-linear code. It is also a subcode of an $RM(r,m)$ code, with $ r \geq s-1$, that can be used for additional random error correction. The encoding requires no mask search and is straightforward based on the description of the recursive construction. The decoding is done in a single attempt and requires almost no additional complexity or latency.

</details>


### [222] [Constructions of Rank-Metric Codes of Small Tensor Rank](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21784)
*Matteo Bonini,Eimear Byrne,Giuseppe Cotardo*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究秩度量码的张量秩下界与构造，提出“张量秩缺陷”概念，并利用代数几何码构造低缺陷的秩度量码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 秩度量码可表示为张量，其张量秩衡量代码分解为秩一张量所需的最小规模。已有 Kruskal 下界及 MTR 码与 MDS 码存在性的关联，但仍需更系统地理解张量秩与相关 Hamming 度量线性码参数之间的关系，并寻找接近最优的小张量秩构造。

Method: 作者建立秩度量码张量秩与关联 Hamming 度量线性码参数之间的新关系，引入张量秩缺陷来度量相对 Kruskal 下界的偏离程度，并借助代数几何码设计具有小张量秩缺陷的秩度量码构造。

Result: 论文得到新的参数关系和下界/结构性结论，并给出基于 AG 码的秩度量码族，这些码具有较小的张量秩缺陷，说明其张量秩接近理论下界。

Conclusion: 该工作拓展了秩度量码张量秩理论，将张量分解、Hamming 度量线性码与代数几何码构造联系起来，为构造接近 MTR 的秩度量码提供了新工具。

Abstract: Rank-metric codes are subspaces of matrices over finite fields endowed with the rank metric and admit a natural tensorial representation. The tensor rank provides a measure of the minimal size of a decomposition of a code into rank-one tensors. Kruskal showed that the tensor rank of a rank-metric code of dimension $k$ and minimum rank distance $d$ is at least $k + d - 1$, and codes meeting this bound with equality are called minimal tensor rank (MTR) codes. It is known from algebraic complexity theory that the existence of an MTR code implies the existence of a maximum distance separable (MDS) code. In this work, we establish new results relating the tensor rank of a rank-metric code to the parameters of associated linear codes in the Hamming metric and introduce the notion of tensor rank defect. We then develop new constructions of rank-metric codes with small tensor rank defect using algebraic geometry (AG) codes.

</details>


### [223] [Near-Field User Location Inference From Far-Field Power Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21815)
*Shima Mashhadi,Tiep M. Hoang,Alireza Vahid*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究利用ELAA近场波束聚焦在焦点外产生的、与用户位置相关的泄漏功率特征，实现仅依赖分布式远场传感器接收功率的被动用户定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 6G中超大孔径阵列可通过近场波束聚焦提升连接规模与频谱效率，但焦点外辐射泄漏通常被视为副作用。作者观察到该泄漏具有随焦点坐标变化的结构化功率分布，因此可作为无需主动测角/测时信息的定位线索。

Method: 论文建立分布式远场传感器仅测量接收功率的统计推断模型，利用非中心卡方分布刻画观测统计特性，并推导贝叶斯Cramér-Rao下界以给出定位误差的理论极限。同时评估两类估计器：基于物理模型的网格搜索估计器，以及具备注意力机制和置换不变性的DeepSet深度学习回归器。

Result: 在视距与多径传播场景下，实验结果表明该被动定位机制可实现可靠的位置推断；随着传感器数量和快照数量增加，定位精度进一步提升。

Conclusion: ELAA近场波束聚焦的焦点外泄漏并非单纯干扰，而可被利用为位置相关的功率指纹，为6G大规模连接场景提供了一种低信息量观测条件下的被动用户定位新范式。

Abstract: Near-field beamfocusing enabled by extremely large-aperture arrays (ELAA) is a promising 6G technique for massive connectivity and high spectrum efficiency. While beamfocusing concentrates energy at an intended user, the radiated field outside the focal point exhibits a structured leakage that varies with the focal-point coordinates. This paper shows that this leakage enables a new form of passive user localization in which distributed far-field sensors measuring only received power can infer the user's location by exploiting this location-dependent power signature. Using the induced noncentral chi-square statistics, we derive a Bayesian Cramér-Rao lower bound (BCRLB) that establishes the fundamental limits of this inference problem. We then evaluate a model-based grid-search estimator and an attention-based permutation-invariant deep learning regressor (DeepSet). Results under both line-of-sight (LoS) and multipath propagation confirm that reliable location inference is feasible, with accuracy improving as more sensors and snapshots are used.

</details>


### [224] [An Information-theoretic Analysis of Edge-reinforced Random Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21853)
*Qinghua,Ding,Venkat Anantharam*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究有限图上边强化随机游走（ERRW）的信息论量，包括熵率、环境分布间KL散度与有限轨迹分布间KL散度，并给出表示公式与收敛界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ERRW可表示为随机环境中的随机游走，其环境律由“magic formula”给出。论文动机是理解ERRW轨迹的统计可区分性，尤其服务于两点假设检验及相关Stein指数，并为身份检验、接近性检验等问题奠定信息论基础。

Method: 利用有限图ERRW的随机环境表示及其结构性质，分析熵率的退火表示；推导不同初始边权诱导的ERRW环境律之间KL散度的闭式表达；进一步比较有限轨迹分布KL散度与环境层面KL散度，建立定量收敛界。

Result: 论文得到ERRW熵率的annealed表示、环境层面KL散度的闭式公式，以及轨迹层面KL散度收敛到环境层面KL散度的定量边界。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明随机环境表示是研究ERRW统计性质的有效工具；所得信息论量能够刻画不同ERRW模型的可区分性，并可用于ERRW相关假设检验问题的理论分析。

Abstract: Reinforced random walks are random walks on graphs whose transition probabilities along edges from a vertex are proportional to the weights of those edges, but where the weight of an edge evolves in a way that depends on the past traversals across it. In an edge-reinforced random walk (ERRW), the weight of an edge increases by $1$ whenever that edge is traversed, in either direction. On a finite graph, an ERRW admits a remarkable representation as a random walk in a random environment. The law of the environment is given by the so-called {\em magic formula}, with this law depending on the initial edge weights. This representation provides a natural route for studying statistical properties of ERRWs.
  This work focuses on various information-theoretic quantities associated with ERRWs on finite graphs, motivated in part by the problem of statistically distinguishing between different ERRW models from observed trajectories. In particular, we study the entropy rate of an ERRW. We also study the Kullback--Leibler divergence (KL divergence) between two ERRW environment laws, and the KL divergence between the corresponding finite-trajectory distributions. Leveraging structural properties of the underlying random environment, we derive an annealed representation of the entropy rate, a closed-form formula for the environment-level KL divergence, and quantitative bounds on the convergence of trajectory-level KL divergence toward environment-level KL divergence.
  These information-theoretic quantities are motivated by the two-point hypothesis testing problem for ERRW trajectories, and in particular by the associated Stein exponent. We also expect them to play a fundamental role in the study of other testing problems for ERRWs, including identity testing and closeness testing.

</details>


### [225] [Finite-Aperture Planar Fluid Antenna Array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22040)
*Zhentian Zhang,Jingyuan Xu,Kai-Kit Wong,Hao Jiang,Zaichen Zhang,Hyundong Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对有限孔径平面流体天线阵列建立解析框架，刻画随机端口几何分布、参数估计精度界以及精度与空间模糊之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要关注流体天线系统的衰落多样性，而由可重构端口位置带来的几何多样性，尤其是在有限孔径平面结构中的影响尚不充分清楚。

Method: 论文推导矩形孔径内均匀随机端口布置下最小端口间距的闭式分布；构建联合俯仰角—方位角估计的通用Cramér-Rao界，并用二维几何惯性矩阵描述端口布局对估计精度的影响；进一步分析几何行列式最大化与旁瓣模糊之间的关系。

Result: 最小端口间距服从Rayleigh分布，其均值随候选端口数M按O(M^{-1})缩放，优于线性阵列的O(M^{-2})；CRB由2×2几何惯性矩阵的行列式和特征结构决定，且该矩阵的迹和行列式对方位观察方向不变；最大化几何行列式会推动端口靠近孔径边界，但会增强旁瓣诱发的空间模糊。

Conclusion: 平面流体天线阵列在二维孔径中具备更有利的几何打包特性，并可通过几何惯性矩阵统一解释角度估计性能；然而，高估计精度与低空间模糊不可同时简单最优，需要进行布局权衡设计。

Abstract: Fluid antenna systems (FASs) are emerging as a reconfigurable-aperture technology that expands physical-layer design beyond fixed, rigid antenna geometries. While the \emph{fading diversity} of FASs -- which exploits spatial channel fluctuations for signal enhancement and interference avoidance -- has been widely studied, the \emph{geometry diversity} created by reconfigurable port placement remains far less understood, particularly for planar architectures under finite-aperture constraints. This paper develops a systematic analytical framework for finite-aperture planar fluid antenna arrays (FAAs). First, we derive a closed-form characterization of the minimum inter-port distance under uniform random placement over a rectangular aperture and show that it follows a Rayleigh law. Its mean scales as $\mathcal{O}(M^{-1})$, in sharp contrast to the $\mathcal{O}(M^{-2})$ behavior in the linear case in which $M$ represents the number of candidate ports, revealing a fundamentally more favorable packing geometry in two dimensions. Secondly, we establish a universal Cramér-Rao bound (CRB) for joint elevation-azimuth estimation, governed by a $2\times 2$ \emph{geometric inertia matrix} whose determinant and eigenstructure fully capture the role of port placement in estimation precision. We further prove that both the trace and determinant of this matrix are invariant to the azimuth look direction. Third, we uncover an intrinsic \emph{precision--ambiguity trade-off}: maximizing the geometric determinant to minimize the CRB drives ports toward the aperture boundary, but simultaneously increases sidelobe-induced spatial ambiguity.

</details>


### [226] [Stacked Intelligent Metasurface-Assisted Fluid Antenna Systems: Outage Probability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22053)
*Anastasios Papazafeiropoulos*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种联合堆叠智能超表面（SIM）与流体天线系统（FAS）的通信模型，并推导中断概率闭式表达，优化SIM相移以降低中断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SIM具备波域信号操控能力，FAS具备空间域信号操控能力。将二者结合有望同时利用波域与空间域自由度，提升通信可靠性与链路性能。

Method: 构建由SIM负责发射、FAS负责接收的联合SIM-FAS通信模型；采用块对角矩阵近似（BDMA）简化分析；推导中断概率的闭式表达式；进一步优化SIM相移以最小化中断概率。

Result: 数值结果验证了所推导解析表达式的准确性，并表明该方案相较传统基准方案具有显著性能增益。

Conclusion: 联合SIM-FAS架构能够有效提升通信系统的可靠性，BDMA为性能分析提供了可处理的近似工具，而SIM相移优化是获得性能提升的关键。

Abstract: Stacked intelligent metasurfaces (SIMs) and fluid antenna systems (FAS) are emerging technologies for wave-domain and spatial signal manipulation, respectively.This letter proposes a novel joint SIM-FAS communication model in which transmission and reception are performed by a SIM and an FAS, respectively. Using the block-diagonal matrix approximation (BDMA), a closed-form expression for the outage probability is derived, and the SIM phase shifts are optimized to minimize outage. Numerical results validate the analytical accuracy and demonstrate substantial performance gains over conventional benchmark schemes.

</details>


### [227] [Fluid RIS (FRIS)-Assisted Index Modulation for 6G Wireless Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22508)
*Xusheng Zhu,Kai-Kit Wong,Sai Xu,Hao Xu,Wen Chen,Hyundong Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出面向接收响应可分性的FRIS空间码本设计视角，用于支持索引调制并降低索引检测错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RIS缺少空间可重构性，而FRIS可通过可切换孔径、图案可重构单元、流体导电材料或可移动表面元素提供更丰富的配置。然而，布局差异并不必然转化为接收端可可靠区分的空间索引；传播、互耦、硬件失真与接收观测会使不同布局产生相似响应。

Method: 文章从“响应感知”角度设计FRIS空间码本：不再仅依据物理布局多样性选择配置，而是依据接收响应域中的可分离性筛选空间索引。同时讨论执行粒度作为设计参数，用于平衡空间多样性、导频开销、互耦鲁棒性和硬件可实现性。

Result: 该工作形成了一套从密集FRIS布局中选择紧凑、可训练、可控制空间索引码本的设计流程，有助于提升索引检测可靠性并降低训练与硬件负担。

Conclusion: FRIS与索引调制结合具有潜力，但关键在于选择接收端可区分的配置集合；响应感知码本设计和合适的执行粒度是未来可编程无线环境中的重要设计原则。

Abstract: Fluid reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (FRIS) extend conventional reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RIS) by adding spatial reconfigurability through switchable apertures, pattern-reconfigurable units, fluidic conductive materials, or movable surface elements. This article studies how FRIS can support index modulation (IM), where information bits select a surface configuration and the receiver detects the index from the induced receiver-side response. A key challenge is that many feasible FRIS layouts do not necessarily lead to many reliable spatial indices. After propagation, mutual coupling, hardware distortion, and receiver observation, different layouts may produce similar receiver-side responses and cause index-detection errors. To address this issue, we present a response-aware design view, in which FRIS spatial codebooks are selected according to response-domain separability rather than layout diversity alone. We also discuss actuation granularity as a practical design knob that balances spatial diversity, pilot overhead, coupling robustness, and hardware feasibility. The resulting workflow helps select compact, trainable, and controllable spatial-index codebooks from dense FRIS layouts, providing design guidance for future programmable wireless environments.

</details>
